Proving begin prop_01: (append (take n xs) (drop n xs)) = xs
prop_01 = VALID (0.01 sec)
{-@prop_01::xs: (List a)->n: Nat->{ (append (take n xs) (drop n xs)) = xs }@-}
prop_01::(List a)->Nat->Proof
prop_01 xs n=
  case n of
    (S n_50) ->
      case xs of
        (Cons xs_70 xs_71) ->
          -- 
          (append (take n xs) (drop n xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_01:n=(S n_50) =>
          (append (take (S n_50) xs) (drop n xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_01:n=(S n_50):xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71) =>
          (append (take (S n_50) (Cons xs_70 xs_71)) (drop n xs))
          ==.
          -- (take (S ?n) (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
          (append (Cons xs_70 (take n_50 xs_71)) (drop n xs))
          ==.
          -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
          (Cons xs_70 (append (take n_50 xs_71) (drop n xs)))
          ==.
          -- prop_01:n=(S n_50) =>
          (Cons xs_70 (append (take n_50 xs_71) (drop (S n_50) xs)))
          ==.
          -- prop_01:n=(S n_50):xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71) =>
          (Cons xs_70 (append (take n_50 xs_71) (drop (S n_50) (Cons xs_70 xs_71))))
          ==.
          -- (drop (S ?n) (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
          (Cons xs_70 (append (take n_50 xs_71) (drop n_50 xs_71)))
          ==.
          -- lemma-(append (take ?n ?xs) (drop ?n ?xs))=?xs =>
          (Cons xs_70 xs_71)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_01:n=(S n_50):xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71)
          xs
          ***
          QED
        (Nil ) ->
          -- 
          (append (take n xs) (drop n xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_01:n=(S n_50) =>
          (append (take (S n_50) xs) (drop n xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_01:n=(S n_50):xs=Nil =>
          (append (take (S n_50) Nil) (drop n xs))
          ==.
          -- (take (S ?n) Nil) =>
          (append Nil (drop n xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_01:n=(S n_50) =>
          (append Nil (drop (S n_50) xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_01:n=(S n_50):xs=Nil =>
          (append Nil (drop (S n_50) Nil))
          ==.
          -- (drop (S ?n) Nil) =>
          (append Nil Nil)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_01:n=(S n_50):xs=Nil
          (append Nil xs)
          ==.
          -- (append Nil ?ys) =>
          xs
          ***
          QED
    (Z ) ->
      -- 
      (append (take n xs) (drop n xs))
      ==.
      -- prop_01:n=Z =>
      (append (take Z xs) (drop n xs))
      ==.
      -- (take Z ?xs) =>
      (append Nil (drop n xs))
      ==.
      -- prop_01:n=Z =>
      (append Nil (drop Z xs))
      ==.
      -- (drop Z ?xs) =>
      (append Nil xs)
      ==.
      -- (append Nil ?ys) =>
      xs
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_02: (add (count n xs) (count n ys)) = (count n (append xs ys))
prop_02 = VALID (0.08 sec)
{-@prop_02::n: Nat->ys: (List Nat)->xs: (List Nat)->{ (add (count n xs) (count n ys)) = (count n (append xs ys)) }@-}
prop_02::Nat->(List Nat)->(List Nat)->Proof
prop_02 n ys xs=
  case n of
    (S n_80) ->
      case xs of
        (Cons xs_100 xs_101) ->
          case g-16 of
            (False ) ->
              -- 
              (add (count n xs) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_02:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101) =>
              (add (count n (Cons xs_100 xs_101)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
              (add (ite (eq n xs_100) (S (count n xs_101)) (count n xs_101)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (add (ite g-16 (S (count n xs_101)) (count n xs_101)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_02:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101):g-16=False =>
              (add (ite False (S (count n xs_101)) (count n xs_101)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
              (add (count n xs_101) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_02:n=(S n_80) =>
              (add (count (S n_80) xs_101) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_02:n=(S n_80) =>
              (add (count (S n_80) xs_101) (count (S n_80) ys))
              ==.
              -- <= lemma-(count (S ?n_80) (append ?xs ?ys))=(add (count (S ?n_80) ?xs) (count (S ?n_80) ?ys))
              (count (S n_80) (append xs_101 ys))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_02:n=(S n_80)
              (count n (append xs_101 ys))
              ==.
              -- <= (ite False ?x ?y)
              (ite False (S (count n (append xs_101 ys))) (count n (append xs_101 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_02:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101):g-16=False
              (ite g-16 (S (count n (append xs_101 ys))) (count n (append xs_101 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= add guard scrutinee
              (ite (eq n xs_100) (S (count n (append xs_101 ys))) (count n (append xs_101 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))
              (count n (Cons xs_100 (append xs_101 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys)
              (count n (append (Cons xs_100 xs_101) ys))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_02:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101)
              (count n (append xs ys))
              ***
              QED
            (True ) ->
              -- 
              (add (count n xs) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_02:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101) =>
              (add (count n (Cons xs_100 xs_101)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
              (add (ite (eq n xs_100) (S (count n xs_101)) (count n xs_101)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (add (ite g-16 (S (count n xs_101)) (count n xs_101)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_02:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101):g-16=True =>
              (add (ite True (S (count n xs_101)) (count n xs_101)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
              (add (S (count n xs_101)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- (add (S ?x) ?y) =>
              (S (add (count n xs_101) (count n ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_02:n=(S n_80) =>
              (S (add (count (S n_80) xs_101) (count n ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_02:n=(S n_80) =>
              (S (add (count (S n_80) xs_101) (count (S n_80) ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= lemma-(count (S ?n_80) (append ?xs ?ys))=(add (count (S ?n_80) ?xs) (count (S ?n_80) ?ys))
              (S (count (S n_80) (append xs_101 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_02:n=(S n_80)
              (S (count n (append xs_101 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= (ite True ?x ?y)
              (ite True (S (count n (append xs_101 ys))) (count n (append xs_101 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_02:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101):g-16=True
              (ite g-16 (S (count n (append xs_101 ys))) (count n (append xs_101 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= add guard scrutinee
              (ite (eq n xs_100) (S (count n (append xs_101 ys))) (count n (append xs_101 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))
              (count n (Cons xs_100 (append xs_101 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys)
              (count n (append (Cons xs_100 xs_101) ys))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_02:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101)
              (count n (append xs ys))
              ***
              QED
        (Nil ) ->
          -- 
          (add (count n xs) (count n ys))
          ==.
          -- prop_02:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil =>
          (add (count n Nil) (count n ys))
          ==.
          -- (count ?x Nil) =>
          (add Z (count n ys))
          ==.
          -- (add Z ?y) =>
          (count n ys)
          ==.
          -- <= (append Nil ?ys)
          (count n (append Nil ys))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_02:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil
          (count n (append xs ys))
          ***
          QED
    (Z ) ->
      case xs of
        (Cons xs_90 xs_91) ->
          case g-15 of
            (False ) ->
              -- 
              (add (count n xs) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_02:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91) =>
              (add (count n (Cons xs_90 xs_91)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
              (add (ite (eq n xs_90) (S (count n xs_91)) (count n xs_91)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (add (ite g-15 (S (count n xs_91)) (count n xs_91)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_02:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91):g-15=False =>
              (add (ite False (S (count n xs_91)) (count n xs_91)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
              (add (count n xs_91) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_02:n=Z =>
              (add (count Z xs_91) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_02:n=Z =>
              (add (count Z xs_91) (count Z ys))
              ==.
              -- <= lemma-(count Z (append ?xs ?ys))=(add (count Z ?xs) (count Z ?ys))
              (count Z (append xs_91 ys))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_02:n=Z
              (count n (append xs_91 ys))
              ==.
              -- <= (ite False ?x ?y)
              (ite False (S (count n (append xs_91 ys))) (count n (append xs_91 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_02:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91):g-15=False
              (ite g-15 (S (count n (append xs_91 ys))) (count n (append xs_91 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= add guard scrutinee
              (ite (eq n xs_90) (S (count n (append xs_91 ys))) (count n (append xs_91 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))
              (count n (Cons xs_90 (append xs_91 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys)
              (count n (append (Cons xs_90 xs_91) ys))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_02:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91)
              (count n (append xs ys))
              ***
              QED
            (True ) ->
              -- 
              (add (count n xs) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_02:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91) =>
              (add (count n (Cons xs_90 xs_91)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
              (add (ite (eq n xs_90) (S (count n xs_91)) (count n xs_91)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (add (ite g-15 (S (count n xs_91)) (count n xs_91)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_02:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91):g-15=True =>
              (add (ite True (S (count n xs_91)) (count n xs_91)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
              (add (S (count n xs_91)) (count n ys))
              ==.
              -- (add (S ?x) ?y) =>
              (S (add (count n xs_91) (count n ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_02:n=Z =>
              (S (add (count Z xs_91) (count n ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_02:n=Z =>
              (S (add (count Z xs_91) (count Z ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= lemma-(count Z (append ?xs ?ys))=(add (count Z ?xs) (count Z ?ys))
              (S (count Z (append xs_91 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_02:n=Z
              (S (count n (append xs_91 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= (ite True ?x ?y)
              (ite True (S (count n (append xs_91 ys))) (count n (append xs_91 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_02:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91):g-15=True
              (ite g-15 (S (count n (append xs_91 ys))) (count n (append xs_91 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= add guard scrutinee
              (ite (eq n xs_90) (S (count n (append xs_91 ys))) (count n (append xs_91 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))
              (count n (Cons xs_90 (append xs_91 ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys)
              (count n (append (Cons xs_90 xs_91) ys))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_02:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91)
              (count n (append xs ys))
              ***
              QED
        (Nil ) ->
          -- 
          (add (count n xs) (count n ys))
          ==.
          -- prop_02:n=Z:xs=Nil =>
          (add (count n Nil) (count n ys))
          ==.
          -- (count ?x Nil) =>
          (add Z (count n ys))
          ==.
          -- (add Z ?y) =>
          (count n ys)
          ==.
          -- <= (append Nil ?ys)
          (count n (append Nil ys))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_02:n=Z:xs=Nil
          (count n (append xs ys))
          ***
          QED

Proving begin prop_03: (leq (count n xs) (count n (append xs ys))) = True
prop_03 = VALID (0.04 sec)
{-@prop_03::n: Nat->xs: (List Nat)->ys: (List Nat)->{ (leq (count n xs) (count n (append xs ys))) = True }@-}
prop_03::Nat->(List Nat)->(List Nat)->Proof
prop_03 n xs ys=
  case n of
    (S n_80) ->
      case xs of
        (Cons xs_100 xs_101) ->
          case g-16 of
            (False ) ->
              -- 
              (leq (count n xs) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101) =>
              (leq (count n (Cons xs_100 xs_101)) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
              (leq (ite (eq n xs_100) (S (count n xs_101)) (count n xs_101)) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (leq (ite g-16 (S (count n xs_101)) (count n xs_101)) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101):g-16=False =>
              (leq (ite False (S (count n xs_101)) (count n xs_101)) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
              (leq (count n xs_101) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=(S n_80) =>
              (leq (count (S n_80) xs_101) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101) =>
              (leq (count (S n_80) xs_101) (count n (append (Cons xs_100 xs_101) ys)))
              ==.
              -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
              (leq (count (S n_80) xs_101) (count n (Cons xs_100 (append xs_101 ys))))
              ==.
              -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
              (leq (count (S n_80) xs_101) (ite (eq n xs_100) (S (count n (append xs_101 ys))) (count n (append xs_101 ys))))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (leq (count (S n_80) xs_101) (ite g-16 (S (count n (append xs_101 ys))) (count n (append xs_101 ys))))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101):g-16=False =>
              (leq (count (S n_80) xs_101) (ite False (S (count n (append xs_101 ys))) (count n (append xs_101 ys))))
              ==.
              -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
              (leq (count (S n_80) xs_101) (count n (append xs_101 ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=(S n_80) =>
              (leq (count (S n_80) xs_101) (count (S n_80) (append xs_101 ys)))
              ==.
              -- lemma-(leq (count (S ?n_80) ?xs) (count (S ?n_80) (append ?xs ?ys)))=True =>
              True
              ***
              QED
            (True ) ->
              -- 
              (leq (count n xs) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101) =>
              (leq (count n (Cons xs_100 xs_101)) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
              (leq (ite (eq n xs_100) (S (count n xs_101)) (count n xs_101)) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (leq (ite g-16 (S (count n xs_101)) (count n xs_101)) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101):g-16=True =>
              (leq (ite True (S (count n xs_101)) (count n xs_101)) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
              (leq (S (count n xs_101)) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101) =>
              (leq (S (count n xs_101)) (count n (append (Cons xs_100 xs_101) ys)))
              ==.
              -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
              (leq (S (count n xs_101)) (count n (Cons xs_100 (append xs_101 ys))))
              ==.
              -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
              (leq (S (count n xs_101)) (ite (eq n xs_100) (S (count n (append xs_101 ys))) (count n (append xs_101 ys))))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (leq (S (count n xs_101)) (ite g-16 (S (count n (append xs_101 ys))) (count n (append xs_101 ys))))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101):g-16=True =>
              (leq (S (count n xs_101)) (ite True (S (count n (append xs_101 ys))) (count n (append xs_101 ys))))
              ==.
              -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
              (leq (S (count n xs_101)) (S (count n (append xs_101 ys))))
              ==.
              -- (leq (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
              (leq (count n xs_101) (count n (append xs_101 ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=(S n_80) =>
              (leq (count (S n_80) xs_101) (count n (append xs_101 ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=(S n_80) =>
              (leq (count (S n_80) xs_101) (count (S n_80) (append xs_101 ys)))

              True
              ***
              QED
        (Nil ) ->
          --

          (leq (count n Nil) (count n (append xs ys)))
          ==.
          -- (count ?x Nil) =>
          (leq Z (count n (append xs ys)))
          ==.
          -- (leq Z ?y) =>
          True
          ***
          QED
    (Z ) ->

              (leq (ite (eq n xs_90) (S (count n xs_91)) (count n xs_91)) (count n (append xs ys)))

              (leq (ite g-15 (S (count n xs_91)) (count n xs_91)) (count n (append xs ys)))

              (leq (ite False (S (count n xs_91)) (count n xs_91)) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
              (leq (count n xs_91) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.

              (leq (count Z xs_91) (count n (append xs ys)))

              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (leq (count Z xs_91) (ite g-15 (S (count n (append xs_91 ys))) (count n (append xs_91 ys))))

              -- prop_03:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91):g-15=False =>
              (leq (count Z xs_91) (ite False (S (count n (append xs_91 ys))) (count n (append xs_91 ys))))
              ==.
              -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
              (leq (count Z xs_91) (count n (append xs_91 ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=Z =>
              (leq (count Z xs_91) (count Z (append xs_91 ys)))
              ==.
              -- lemma-(leq (count Z ?xs) (count Z (append ?xs ?ys)))=True =>
              True
              ***
              QED
            (True ) ->
              -- 
              (leq (count n xs) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91) =>
              (leq (count n (Cons xs_90 xs_91)) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
              (leq (ite (eq n xs_90) (S (count n xs_91)) (count n xs_91)) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (leq (ite g-15 (S (count n xs_91)) (count n xs_91)) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91):g-15=True =>
              (leq (ite True (S (count n xs_91)) (count n xs_91)) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
              (leq (S (count n xs_91)) (count n (append xs ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91) =>
              (leq (S (count n xs_91)) (count n (append (Cons xs_90 xs_91) ys)))
              ==.
              -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
              (leq (S (count n xs_91)) (count n (Cons xs_90 (append xs_91 ys))))
              ==.
              -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
              (leq (S (count n xs_91)) (ite (eq n xs_90) (S (count n (append xs_91 ys))) (count n (append xs_91 ys))))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (leq (S (count n xs_91)) (ite g-15 (S (count n (append xs_91 ys))) (count n (append xs_91 ys))))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91):g-15=True =>
              (leq (S (count n xs_91)) (ite True (S (count n (append xs_91 ys))) (count n (append xs_91 ys))))
              ==.
              -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
              (leq (S (count n xs_91)) (S (count n (append xs_91 ys))))
              ==.
              -- (leq (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
              (leq (count n xs_91) (count n (append xs_91 ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=Z =>
              (leq (count Z xs_91) (count n (append xs_91 ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_03:n=Z =>
              (leq (count Z xs_91) (count Z (append xs_91 ys)))
              ==.
              -- lemma-(leq (count Z ?xs) (count Z (append ?xs ?ys)))=True =>
              True
              ***
              QED
        (Nil ) ->
          -- 
          (leq (count n xs) (count n (append xs ys)))
          ==.
          -- prop_03:n=Z:xs=Nil =>
          (leq (count n Nil) (count n (append xs ys)))
          ==.
          -- (count ?x Nil) =>
          (leq Z (count n (append xs ys)))
          ==.
          -- (leq Z ?y) =>
          True
          ***
          QED

Proving begin prop_09: (sub (sub i j) k) = (sub i (add j k))
prop_09 = VALID (0.01 sec)
{-@prop_09::k: Nat->j: Nat->i: Nat->{ (sub (sub i j) k) = (sub i (add j k)) }@-}
prop_09::Nat->Nat->Nat->Proof
prop_09 k j i=
  case i of
    (S i_70) ->
      case j of
        (S j_90) ->
          -- 
          (sub (sub i j) k)
          ==.
          -- prop_09:i=(S i_70) =>
          (sub (sub (S i_70) j) k)
          ==.
          -- prop_09:i=(S i_70):j=(S j_90) =>
          (sub (sub (S i_70) (S j_90)) k)
          ==.
          -- (sub (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
          (sub (sub i_70 j_90) k)
          ==.
          -- lemma-(sub (sub ?i ?j) ?k)=(sub ?i (add ?j ?k)) =>
          (sub i_70 (add j_90 k))
          ==.
          -- <= (sub (S ?x) (S ?y))
          (sub (S i_70) (S (add j_90 k)))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_09:i=(S i_70)
          (sub i (S (add j_90 k)))
          ==.
          -- <= (add (S ?x) ?y)
          (sub i (add (S j_90) k))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_09:i=(S i_70):j=(S j_90)
          (sub i (add j k))
          ***
          QED
        (Z ) ->
          -- 
          (sub (sub i j) k)
          ==.
          -- prop_09:i=(S i_70):j=Z =>
          (sub (sub i Z) k)
          ==.
          -- (sub ?x Z) =>
          (sub i k)
          ==.
          -- <= (add Z ?y)
          (sub i (add Z k))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_09:i=(S i_70):j=Z
          (sub i (add j k))
          ***
          QED
    (Z ) ->
      -- 
      (sub (sub i j) k)
      ==.
      -- prop_09:i=Z =>
      (sub (sub Z j) k)
      ==.
      -- (sub Z ?y) =>
      (sub Z k)
      ==.
      -- (sub Z ?y) =>
      Z
      ==.
      -- <= (sub Z ?y)
      (sub Z (add j k))
      ==.
      -- <= prop_09:i=Z
      (sub i (add j k))
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_12: (drop n (map f xs)) = (map f (drop n xs))
prop_12 = VALID (0.01 sec)
{-@prop_12::xs: (List a)->f: (-> a b)->n: Nat->{ (drop n (map f xs)) = (map f (drop n xs)) }@-}
prop_12::(List a)->(-> a b)->Nat->Proof
prop_12 xs f n=
  case n of
    (S n_70) ->
      case xs of
        (Cons xs_90 xs_91) ->
          -- 
          (drop n (map f xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_12:n=(S n_70) =>
          (drop (S n_70) (map f xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_12:n=(S n_70):xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91) =>
          (drop (S n_70) (map f (Cons xs_90 xs_91)))
          ==.
          -- (map ?f (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
          (drop (S n_70) (Cons (($) f xs_90) (map f xs_91)))
          ==.
          -- (drop (S ?n) (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
          (drop n_70 (map f xs_91))
          ==.
          -- <= lemma-(map ?f (drop ?n ?xs))=(drop ?n (map ?f ?xs))
          (map f (drop n_70 xs_91))
          ==.
          -- <= (drop (S ?n) (Cons ?x ?xs))
          (map f (drop (S n_70) (Cons xs_90 xs_91)))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_12:n=(S n_70)
          (map f (drop n (Cons xs_90 xs_91)))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_12:n=(S n_70):xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91)
          (map f (drop n xs))
          ***
          QED
        (Nil ) ->
          -- 
          (drop n (map f xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_12:n=(S n_70):xs=Nil =>
          (drop n (map f Nil))
          ==.
          -- (map ?f Nil) =>
          (drop n Nil)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_12:n=(S n_70):xs=Nil
          (drop n xs)
          ==.
          -- prop_12:n=(S n_70) =>
          (drop (S n_70) xs)
          ==.
          -- prop_12:n=(S n_70):xs=Nil =>
          (drop (S n_70) Nil)
          ==.
          -- (drop (S ?n) Nil) =>
          Nil
          ==.
          -- <= (map ?f Nil)
          (map f Nil)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_12:n=(S n_70):xs=Nil
          (map f xs)
          ==.
          -- prop_12:n=(S n_70):xs=Nil =>
          (map f Nil)
          ==.
          -- <= (drop (S ?n) Nil)
          (map f (drop (S n_70) Nil))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_12:n=(S n_70)
          (map f (drop n Nil))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_12:n=(S n_70):xs=Nil
          (map f (drop n xs))
          ***
          QED
    (Z ) ->
      -- 
      (drop n (map f xs))
      ==.
      -- prop_12:n=Z =>
      (drop Z (map f xs))
      ==.
      -- (drop Z ?xs) =>
      (map f xs)
      ==.
      -- <= (drop Z ?xs)
      (map f (drop Z xs))
      ==.
      -- <= prop_12:n=Z
      (map f (drop n xs))
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_14: (filter p (append xs ys)) = (append (filter p xs) (filter p ys))
prop_14 = VALID (0.03 sec)
{-@prop_14::p: (-> a Bool)->ys: (List a)->xs: (List a)->{ (filter p (append xs ys)) = (append (filter p xs) (filter p ys)) }@-}
prop_14::(-> a Bool)->(List a)->(List a)->Proof
prop_14 p ys xs=
  case xs of
    (Cons xs_80 xs_81) ->
      case g-11 of
        (False ) ->
          -- 
          (filter p (append xs ys))
          ==.
          -- prop_14:xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81) =>
          (filter p (append (Cons xs_80 xs_81) ys))
          ==.
          -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
          (filter p (Cons xs_80 (append xs_81 ys)))
          ==.
          -- (filter ?p (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
          (ite (($) p xs_80) (Cons xs_80 (filter p (append xs_81 ys))) (filter p (append xs_81 ys)))
          ==.
          -- add guard scrutinee =>
          (ite g-11 (Cons xs_80 (filter p (append xs_81 ys))) (filter p (append xs_81 ys)))
          ==.
          -- prop_14:xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81):g-11=False =>
          (ite False (Cons xs_80 (filter p (append xs_81 ys))) (filter p (append xs_81 ys)))
          ==.
          -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
          (filter p (append xs_81 ys))
          ==.
          -- lemma-(filter ?p (append ?xs ?ys))=(append (filter ?p ?xs) (filter ?p ?ys)) =>
          (append (filter p xs_81) (filter p ys))
          ==.
          -- <= (ite False ?x ?y)
          (append (ite False (Cons xs_80 (filter p xs_81)) (filter p xs_81)) (filter p ys))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_14:xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81):g-11=False
          (append (ite g-11 (Cons xs_80 (filter p xs_81)) (filter p xs_81)) (filter p ys))
          ==.
          -- <= add guard scrutinee
          (append (ite (($) p xs_80) (Cons xs_80 (filter p xs_81)) (filter p xs_81)) (filter p ys))
          ==.
          -- <= (filter ?p (Cons ?x ?xs))
          (append (filter p (Cons xs_80 xs_81)) (filter p ys))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_14:xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81)
          (append (filter p xs) (filter p ys))
          ***
          QED
        (True ) ->
          -- 
          (filter p (append xs ys))
          ==.
          -- prop_14:xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81) =>
          (filter p (append (Cons xs_80 xs_81) ys))
          ==.
          -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
          (filter p (Cons xs_80 (append xs_81 ys)))
          ==.
          -- (filter ?p (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
          (ite (($) p xs_80) (Cons xs_80 (filter p (append xs_81 ys))) (filter p (append xs_81 ys)))
          ==.
          -- add guard scrutinee =>
          (ite g-11 (Cons xs_80 (filter p (append xs_81 ys))) (filter p (append xs_81 ys)))
          ==.
          -- prop_14:xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81):g-11=True =>
          (ite True (Cons xs_80 (filter p (append xs_81 ys))) (filter p (append xs_81 ys)))
          ==.
          -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
          (Cons xs_80 (filter p (append xs_81 ys)))
          ==.
          -- lemma-(filter ?p (append ?xs ?ys))=(append (filter ?p ?xs) (filter ?p ?ys)) =>
          (Cons xs_80 (append (filter p xs_81) (filter p ys)))
          ==.
          -- <= (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys)
          (append (Cons xs_80 (filter p xs_81)) (filter p ys))
          ==.
          -- <= (ite True ?x ?y)
          (append (ite True (Cons xs_80 (filter p xs_81)) (filter p xs_81)) (filter p ys))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_14:xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81):g-11=True
          (append (ite g-11 (Cons xs_80 (filter p xs_81)) (filter p xs_81)) (filter p ys))
          ==.
          -- <= add guard scrutinee
          (append (ite (($) p xs_80) (Cons xs_80 (filter p xs_81)) (filter p xs_81)) (filter p ys))
          ==.
          -- <= (filter ?p (Cons ?x ?xs))
          (append (filter p (Cons xs_80 xs_81)) (filter p ys))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_14:xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81)
          (append (filter p xs) (filter p ys))
          ***
          QED
    (Nil ) ->
      -- 
      (filter p (append xs ys))
      ==.
      -- prop_14:xs=Nil =>
      (filter p (append Nil ys))
      ==.
      -- (append Nil ?ys) =>
      (filter p ys)
      ==.
      -- <= (append Nil ?ys)
      (append Nil (filter p ys))
      ==.
      -- <= (filter ?p Nil)
      (append (filter p Nil) (filter p ys))
      ==.
      -- <= prop_14:xs=Nil
      (append (filter p xs) (filter p ys))
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_15: (len (ins x xs)) = (S (len xs))
prop_15 = VALID (0.03 sec)
{-@prop_15::xs: (List Nat)->x: Nat->{ (len (ins x xs)) = (S (len xs)) }@-}
prop_15::(List Nat)->Nat->Proof
prop_15 xs x=
  case x of
    (S x_60) ->
      case xs of
        (Cons xs_80 xs_81) ->
          case g-14 of
            (False ) ->
              -- 
              (len (ins x xs))
              ==.
              -- prop_15:x=(S x_60):xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81) =>
              (len (ins x (Cons xs_80 xs_81)))
              ==.
              -- (ins ?n (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
              (len (ite (lt x xs_80) (Cons x (Cons xs_80 xs_81)) (Cons xs_80 (ins x xs_81))))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_15:x=(S x_60):xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81)
              (len (ite (lt x xs_80) (Cons x xs) (Cons xs_80 (ins x xs_81))))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (len (ite g-14 (Cons x xs) (Cons xs_80 (ins x xs_81))))
              ==.
              -- prop_15:x=(S x_60):xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81):g-14=False =>
              (len (ite False (Cons x xs) (Cons xs_80 (ins x xs_81))))
              ==.
              -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
              (len (Cons xs_80 (ins x xs_81)))
              ==.
              -- (len (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
              (S (len (ins x xs_81)))
              ==.
              -- prop_15:x=(S x_60) =>
              (S (len (ins (S x_60) xs_81)))
              ==.
              -- lemma-(len (ins (S ?x_60) ?xs))=(S (len ?xs)) =>
              (S (S (len xs_81)))
              ==.
              -- <= (len (Cons ?x ?xs))
              (S (len (Cons xs_80 xs_81)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_15:x=(S x_60):xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81)
              (S (len xs))
              ***
              QED
            (True ) ->
              -- 
              (len (ins x xs))
              ==.
              -- prop_15:x=(S x_60):xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81) =>
              (len (ins x (Cons xs_80 xs_81)))
              ==.
              -- (ins ?n (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
              (len (ite (lt x xs_80) (Cons x (Cons xs_80 xs_81)) (Cons xs_80 (ins x xs_81))))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_15:x=(S x_60):xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81)
              (len (ite (lt x xs_80) (Cons x xs) (Cons xs_80 (ins x xs_81))))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (len (ite g-14 (Cons x xs) (Cons xs_80 (ins x xs_81))))
              ==.
              -- prop_15:x=(S x_60):xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81):g-14=True =>
              (len (ite True (Cons x xs) (Cons xs_80 (ins x xs_81))))
              ==.
              -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
              (len (Cons x xs))
              ==.
              -- (len (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
              (S (len xs))
              ***
              QED
        (Nil ) ->
          -- 
          (len (ins x xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_15:x=(S x_60):xs=Nil =>
          (len (ins x Nil))
          ==.
          -- (ins ?n Nil) =>
          (len (Cons x Nil))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_15:x=(S x_60):xs=Nil
          (len (Cons x xs))
          ==.
          -- (len (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
          (S (len xs))
          ***
          QED
    (Z ) ->
      case xs of
        (Cons xs_70 xs_71) ->
          case g-13 of
            (False ) ->
              --

              ==.
              -- prop_15:x=Z:xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71) =>

              -- (ins ?n (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
              (len (ite (lt x xs_70) (Cons x (Cons xs_70 xs_71)) (Cons xs_70 (ins x xs_71))))

              (len (ite (lt x xs_70) (Cons x xs) (Cons xs_70 (ins x xs_71))))

              (len (ite False (Cons x xs) (Cons xs_70 (ins x xs_71))))

              -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
              (len (Cons xs_70 (ins x xs_71)))
              ==.
              -- (len (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
              (S (len (ins x xs_71)))
              ==.

              (S (len (ins Z xs_71)))

              -- <= lemma-(S (len ?xs))=(len (ins Z ?xs))

              (S (len xs))
              ***
              QED
            (True ) ->
              --

              ==.

          ==.
          -- (len (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>

          ***
          QED

Proving begin prop_17: (leq n Z) = (eq n Z)
prop_17 = VALID (0.00 sec)
{-@prop_17::n: Nat->{ (leq n Z) = (eq n Z) }@-}
prop_17::Nat->Proof
prop_17 n=
  case n of
    (S n_40) ->
      -- 
      (leq n Z)
      ==.
      -- prop_17:n=(S n_40) =>
      (leq (S n_40) Z)
      ==.
      -- (leq (S ?x) Z) =>
      False
      ==.
      -- <= (eq (S ?x) Z)
      (eq (S n_40) Z)
      ==.
      -- <= prop_17:n=(S n_40)
      (eq n Z)
      ***
      QED
    (Z ) ->
      -- 
      (leq n Z)
      ==.
      -- prop_17:n=Z =>
      (leq Z Z)
      ==.
      -- <= prop_17:n=Z
      (leq Z n)
      ==.
      -- (leq Z ?y) =>
      True
      ==.
      -- <= (eq Z Z)
      (eq Z Z)
      ==.
      -- <= prop_17:n=Z
      (eq n Z)
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_18: (lt i (S (add i m))) = True
prop_18 = VALID (0.00 sec)
{-@prop_18::i: Nat->m: Nat->{ (lt i (S (add i m))) = True }@-}
prop_18::Nat->Nat->Proof
prop_18 i m=
  case i of
    (S i_60) ->
      -- 
      (lt i (S (add i m)))
      ==.
      -- prop_18:i=(S i_60) =>
      (lt (S i_60) (S (add i m)))
      ==.
      -- (lt (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
      (lt i_60 (add i m))
      ==.
      -- prop_18:i=(S i_60) =>
      (lt i_60 (add (S i_60) m))
      ==.
      -- (add (S ?x) ?y) =>
      (lt i_60 (S (add i_60 m)))
      ==.
      -- lemma-(lt ?i (S (add ?i ?m)))=True =>
      True
      ***
      QED
    (Z ) ->
      -- 
      (lt i (S (add i m)))
      ==.
      -- prop_18:i=Z =>
      (lt Z (S (add i m)))
      ==.
      -- (lt Z (S ?y)) =>
      True
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_19: (len (drop n xs)) = (sub (len xs) n)
prop_19 = VALID (0.01 sec)
{-@prop_19::n: Nat->xs: (List a)->{ (len (drop n xs)) = (sub (len xs) n) }@-}
prop_19::Nat->(List a)->Proof
prop_19 n xs=
  case n of
    (S n_60) ->
      case xs of
        (Cons xs_80 xs_81) ->
          -- 
          (len (drop n xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_19:n=(S n_60) =>
          (len (drop (S n_60) xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_19:n=(S n_60):xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81) =>
          (len (drop (S n_60) (Cons xs_80 xs_81)))
          ==.
          -- (drop (S ?n) (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
          (len (drop n_60 xs_81))
          ==.
          -- lemma-(len (drop ?n ?xs))=(sub (len ?xs) ?n) =>
          (sub (len xs_81) n_60)
          ==.
          -- <= (sub (S ?x) (S ?y))
          (sub (S (len xs_81)) (S n_60))
          ==.
          -- <= (len (Cons ?x ?xs))
          (sub (len (Cons xs_80 xs_81)) (S n_60))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_19:n=(S n_60):xs=(Cons xs_80 xs_81)
          (sub (len xs) (S n_60))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_19:n=(S n_60)
          (sub (len xs) n)
          ***
          QED
        (Nil ) ->
          -- 
          (len (drop n xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_19:n=(S n_60) =>
          (len (drop (S n_60) xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_19:n=(S n_60):xs=Nil =>
          (len (drop (S n_60) Nil))
          ==.
          -- (drop (S ?n) Nil) =>
          (len Nil)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_19:n=(S n_60):xs=Nil
          (len xs)
          ==.
          -- prop_19:n=(S n_60):xs=Nil =>
          (len Nil)
          ==.
          -- (len Nil) =>
          Z
          ==.
          -- <= (sub Z ?y)
          (sub Z n)
          ==.
          -- <= (len Nil)
          (sub (len Nil) n)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_19:n=(S n_60):xs=Nil
          (sub (len xs) n)
          ***
          QED
    (Z ) ->
      -- 
      (len (drop n xs))
      ==.
      -- prop_19:n=Z =>
      (len (drop Z xs))
      ==.
      -- (drop Z ?xs) =>
      (len xs)
      ==.
      -- <= (sub ?x Z)
      (sub (len xs) Z)
      ==.
      -- <= prop_19:n=Z
      (sub (len xs) n)
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_22: (max (max a b) c) = (max a (max b c))
prop_22 = VALID (0.01 sec)
{-@prop_22::a: Nat->b: Nat->c: Nat->{ (max (max a b) c) = (max a (max b c)) }@-}
prop_22::Nat->Nat->Nat->Proof
prop_22 a b c=
  case a of
    (S a_70) ->
      case b of
        (S b_90) ->
          case c of
            (S c_130) ->
              -- 
              (max (max a b) c)
              ==.
              -- prop_22:a=(S a_70) =>
              (max (max (S a_70) b) c)
              ==.
              -- prop_22:a=(S a_70):b=(S b_90) =>
              (max (max (S a_70) (S b_90)) c)
              ==.
              -- (max (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
              (max (S (max a_70 b_90)) c)
              ==.
              -- prop_22:a=(S a_70):b=(S b_90):c=(S c_130) =>
              (max (S (max a_70 b_90)) (S c_130))
              ==.
              -- (max (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
              (S (max (max a_70 b_90) c_130))
              ==.
              -- lemma-(max (max ?a ?b) ?c)=(max ?a (max ?b ?c)) =>
              (S (max a_70 (max b_90 c_130)))
              ==.
              -- <= (max (S ?x) (S ?y))
              (max (S a_70) (S (max b_90 c_130)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_22:a=(S a_70)
              (max a (S (max b_90 c_130)))
              ==.
              -- <= (max (S ?x) (S ?y))
              (max a (max (S b_90) (S c_130)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_22:a=(S a_70):b=(S b_90)
              (max a (max b (S c_130)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_22:a=(S a_70):b=(S b_90):c=(S c_130)
              (max a (max b c))
              ***
              QED
            (Z ) ->
              -- 
              (max (max a b) c)
              ==.
              -- prop_22:a=(S a_70):b=(S b_90):c=Z =>
              (max (max a b) Z)
              ==.
              -- (max ?x Z) =>
              (max a b)
              ==.
              -- <= (max ?x Z)
              (max a (max b Z))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_22:a=(S a_70):b=(S b_90):c=Z
              (max a (max b c))
              ***
              QED
        (Z ) ->
          -- 
          (max (max a b) c)
          ==.
          -- prop_22:a=(S a_70):b=Z =>
          (max (max a Z) c)
          ==.
          -- (max ?x Z) =>
          (max a c)
          ==.
          -- <= (max Z ?y)
          (max a (max Z c))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_22:a=(S a_70):b=Z
          (max a (max b c))
          ***
          QED
    (Z ) ->
      -- 
      (max (max a b) c)
      ==.
      -- prop_22:a=Z =>
      (max (max Z b) c)
      ==.
      -- (max Z ?y) =>
      (max b c)
      ==.
      -- <= (max Z ?y)
      (max Z (max b c))
      ==.
      -- <= prop_22:a=Z
      (max a (max b c))
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_23: (max a b) = (max b a)
prop_23 = VALID (0.00 sec)
{-@prop_23::b: Nat->a: Nat->{ (max a b) = (max b a) }@-}
prop_23::Nat->Nat->Proof
prop_23 b a=
  case a of
    (S a_40) ->
      case b of
        (S b_60) ->
          -- 
          (max a b)
          ==.
          -- prop_23:a=(S a_40) =>
          (max (S a_40) b)
          ==.
          -- prop_23:a=(S a_40):b=(S b_60) =>
          (max (S a_40) (S b_60))
          ==.
          -- (max (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
          (S (max a_40 b_60))
          ==.
          -- lemma-(max ?a ?b)=(max ?b ?a) =>
          (S (max b_60 a_40))
          ==.
          -- <= (max (S ?x) (S ?y))
          (max (S b_60) (S a_40))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_23:a=(S a_40):b=(S b_60)
          (max b (S a_40))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_23:a=(S a_40)
          (max b a)
          ***
          QED
        (Z ) ->
          -- 
          (max a b)
          ==.
          -- prop_23:a=(S a_40):b=Z =>
          (max a Z)
          ==.
          -- (max ?x Z) =>
          a
          ==.
          -- <= (max Z ?y)
          (max Z a)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_23:a=(S a_40):b=Z
          (max b a)
          ***
          QED
    (Z ) ->
      -- 
      (max a b)
      ==.
      -- prop_23:a=Z =>
      (max Z b)
      ==.
      -- (max Z ?y) =>
      b
      ==.
      -- <= (max ?x Z)
      (max b Z)
      ==.
      -- <= prop_23:a=Z
      (max b a)
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_24: (eq (max a b) a) = (leq b a)
prop_24 = VALID (0.01 sec)
{-@prop_24::a: Nat->b: Nat->{ (eq (max a b) a) = (leq b a) }@-}
prop_24::Nat->Nat->Proof
prop_24 a b=
  case a of
    (S a_50) ->
      case b of
        (S b_70) ->
          -- 
          (eq (max a b) a)
          ==.
          -- prop_24:a=(S a_50) =>
          (eq (max (S a_50) b) a)
          ==.
          -- prop_24:a=(S a_50):b=(S b_70) =>
          (eq (max (S a_50) (S b_70)) a)
          ==.
          -- (max (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
          (eq (S (max a_50 b_70)) a)
          ==.
          -- prop_24:a=(S a_50) =>
          (eq (S (max a_50 b_70)) (S a_50))
          ==.
          -- (eq (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
          (eq (max a_50 b_70) a_50)
          ==.
          -- <= lemma-(leq ?b ?a)=(eq (max ?a ?b) ?a)
          (leq b_70 a_50)
          ==.
          -- <= (leq (S ?x) (S ?y))
          (leq (S b_70) (S a_50))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_24:a=(S a_50):b=(S b_70)
          (leq b (S a_50))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_24:a=(S a_50)
          (leq b a)
          ***
          QED
        (Z ) ->
          case a_50 of
            (S a_50_110) ->
              -- 
              (eq (max a b) a)
              ==.
              -- prop_24:a=(S a_50):b=Z =>
              (eq (max a Z) a)
              ==.
              -- (max ?x Z) =>
              (eq a a)
              ==.
              -- prop_24:a=(S a_50) =>
              (eq (S a_50) a)
              ==.
              -- prop_24:a=(S a_50) =>
              (eq (S a_50) (S a_50))
              ==.
              -- (eq (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
              (eq a_50 a_50)
              ==.
              -- prop_24:a=(S a_50):b=Z:a_50=(S a_50_110) =>
              (eq (S a_50_110) a_50)
              ==.
              -- prop_24:a=(S a_50):b=Z:a_50=(S a_50_110) =>
              (eq (S a_50_110) (S a_50_110))
              ==.
              -- lemma-(eq (S ?a_50) (S ?a_50))=True =>
              True
              ==.
              -- <= (leq Z ?y)
              (leq Z a)
              ==.
              -- <= prop_24:a=(S a_50):b=Z
              (leq b a)
              ***
              QED
            (Z ) ->
              -- 
              (eq (max a b) a)
              ==.
              -- prop_24:a=(S a_50):b=Z =>
              (eq (max a Z) a)
              ==.
              -- (max ?x Z) =>
              (eq a a)
              ==.
              -- prop_24:a=(S a_50) =>
              (eq (S a_50) a)
              ==.
              -- prop_24:a=(S a_50) =>
              (eq (S a_50) (S a_50))
              ==.
              -- (eq (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
              (eq a_50 a_50)
              ==.
              -- prop_24:a=(S a_50):b=Z:a_50=Z =>
              (eq Z a_50)
              ==.
              -- prop_24:a=(S a_50):b=Z:a_50=Z =>
              (eq Z Z)
              ==.
              -- (eq Z Z) =>
              True
              ==.
              -- <= (leq Z ?y)
              (leq Z a)
              ==.
              -- <= prop_24:a=(S a_50):b=Z
              (leq b a)
              ***
              QED
    (Z ) ->
      case b of
        (S b_70) ->
          -- 
          (eq (max a b) a)
          ==.
          -- prop_24:a=Z =>
          (eq (max Z b) a)
          ==.
          -- (max Z ?y) =>
          (eq b a)
          ==.
          -- prop_24:a=Z:b=(S b_70) =>
          (eq (S b_70) a)
          ==.
          -- prop_24:a=Z =>
          (eq (S b_70) Z)
          ==.
          -- (eq (S ?x) Z) =>
          False
          ==.
          -- <= (leq (S ?x) Z)
          (leq (S b_70) Z)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_24:a=Z:b=(S b_70)
          (leq b Z)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_24:a=Z
          (leq b a)
          ***
          QED

          ==.

prop_25 = VALID (0.01 sec)
{-@prop_25::b: Nat->a: Nat->{ (eq (max a b) b) = (leq a b) }@-}
prop_25::Nat->Nat->Proof
prop_25 b a=
  case a of
    (S a_50) ->
      case b of
        (S b_70) ->
          -- 
          (eq (max a b) b)
          ==.
          -- prop_25:a=(S a_50) =>
          (eq (max (S a_50) b) b)
          ==.
          -- prop_25:a=(S a_50):b=(S b_70) =>
          (eq (max (S a_50) (S b_70)) b)
          ==.
          -- (max (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
          (eq (S (max a_50 b_70)) b)
          ==.

          (eq (S (max a_50 b_70)) (S b_70))
          ==.

          (eq (max a_50 b_70) b_70)

          (leq a_50 b_70)

          (leq (S a_50) (S b_70))

          (leq a (S b_70))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_25:a=(S a_50):b=(S b_70)
          (leq a b)
          ***
          QED

          -- 
          (eq (max a b) b)
          ==.
          -- prop_25:a=(S a_50):b=Z =>
          (eq (max a Z) b)
          ==.
          -- (max ?x Z) =>
          (eq a b)
          ==.

          (eq (S a_50) b)

          False
          ==.

          (leq (S a_50) Z)

          (leq a Z)

          (leq a b)
          ***
          QED
    (Z ) ->
      case b of
        (S b_80) ->
          -- 
          (eq (max a b) b)
          ==.
          -- prop_25:a=Z =>
          (eq (max Z b) b)
          ==.
          -- (max Z ?y) =>
          (eq b b)
          ==.
          -- prop_25:a=Z:b=(S b_80) =>
          (eq (S b_80) b)
          ==.
          -- prop_25:a=Z:b=(S b_80) =>
          (eq (S b_80) (S b_80))
          ==.
          -- (eq (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
          (eq b_80 b_80)
          ==.
          -- lemma-(eq ?b ?b)=True =>
          True
          ==.
          -- <= (leq Z ?y)
          (leq Z b)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_25:a=Z
          (leq a b)
          ***
          QED

Proving begin prop_31: (min (min a b) c) = (min a (min b c))
prop_31 = VALID (0.02 sec)
{-@prop_31::a: Nat->b: Nat->c: Nat->{ (min (min a b) c) = (min a (min b c)) }@-}
prop_31::Nat->Nat->Nat->Proof
prop_31 a b c=
  case a of
    (S a_70) ->
      case b of
        (S b_90) ->
          case c of
            (S c_130) ->
              -- 
              (min (min a b) c)
              ==.
              -- prop_31:a=(S a_70) =>
              (min (min (S a_70) b) c)
              ==.
              -- prop_31:a=(S a_70):b=(S b_90) =>
              (min (min (S a_70) (S b_90)) c)
              ==.
              -- (min (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
              (min (S (min a_70 b_90)) c)
              ==.
              -- prop_31:a=(S a_70):b=(S b_90):c=(S c_130) =>
              (min (S (min a_70 b_90)) (S c_130))
              ==.
              -- (min (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
              (S (min (min a_70 b_90) c_130))
              ==.
              -- lemma-(min (min ?a ?b) ?c)=(min ?a (min ?b ?c)) =>
              (S (min a_70 (min b_90 c_130)))
              ==.
              -- <= (min (S ?x) (S ?y))
              (min (S a_70) (S (min b_90 c_130)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_31:a=(S a_70)
              (min a (S (min b_90 c_130)))
              ==.
              -- <= (min (S ?x) (S ?y))
              (min a (min (S b_90) (S c_130)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_31:a=(S a_70):b=(S b_90)
              (min a (min b (S c_130)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_31:a=(S a_70):b=(S b_90):c=(S c_130)
              (min a (min b c))
              ***
              QED
            (Z ) ->
              -- 
              (min (min a b) c)
              ==.
              -- prop_31:a=(S a_70):b=(S b_90):c=Z =>
              (min (min a b) Z)
              ==.
              -- (min ?x Z) =>
              Z
              ==.
              -- <= (min ?x Z)
              (min a Z)
              ==.
              -- <= (min ?x Z)
              (min a (min b Z))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_31:a=(S a_70):b=(S b_90):c=Z
              (min a (min b c))
              ***
              QED
        (Z ) ->
          -- 
          (min (min a b) c)
          ==.
          -- prop_31:a=(S a_70):b=Z =>
          (min (min a Z) c)
          ==.
          -- (min ?x Z) =>
          (min Z c)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_31:a=(S a_70):b=Z
          (min b c)
          ==.
          -- prop_31:a=(S a_70):b=Z =>
          (min Z c)
          ==.
          -- (min Z ?y) =>
          Z
          ==.
          -- <= (min ?x Z)
          (min a Z)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_31:a=(S a_70):b=Z
          (min a b)
          ==.
          -- prop_31:a=(S a_70):b=Z =>
          (min a Z)
          ==.
          -- <= (min Z ?y)
          (min a (min Z c))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_31:a=(S a_70):b=Z
          (min a (min b c))
          ***
          QED
    (Z ) ->
      -- 
      (min (min a b) c)
      ==.
      -- prop_31:a=Z =>
      (min (min Z b) c)
      ==.
      -- (min Z ?y) =>
      (min Z c)
      ==.
      -- (min Z ?y) =>
      Z
      ==.
      -- <= (min Z ?y)
      (min Z (min b c))
      ==.
      -- <= prop_31:a=Z
      (min a (min b c))
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_32: (min a b) = (min b a)
prop_32 = VALID (0.00 sec)
{-@prop_32::a: Nat->b: Nat->{ (min a b) = (min b a) }@-}
prop_32::Nat->Nat->Proof
prop_32 a b=
  case a of
    (S a_40) ->
      case b of
        (S b_60) ->
          -- 
          (min a b)
          ==.
          -- prop_32:a=(S a_40) =>
          (min (S a_40) b)
          ==.
          -- prop_32:a=(S a_40):b=(S b_60) =>
          (min (S a_40) (S b_60))
          ==.
          -- (min (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
          (S (min a_40 b_60))
          ==.
          -- lemma-(min ?a ?b)=(min ?b ?a) =>
          (S (min b_60 a_40))
          ==.
          -- <= (min (S ?x) (S ?y))
          (min (S b_60) (S a_40))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_32:a=(S a_40):b=(S b_60)
          (min b (S a_40))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_32:a=(S a_40)
          (min b a)
          ***
          QED
        (Z ) ->
          -- 
          (min a b)
          ==.
          -- prop_32:a=(S a_40):b=Z =>
          (min a Z)
          ==.
          -- (min ?x Z) =>
          Z
          ==.
          -- <= (min Z ?y)
          (min Z a)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_32:a=(S a_40):b=Z
          (min b a)
          ***
          QED
    (Z ) ->
      -- 
      (min a b)
      ==.
      -- prop_32:a=Z =>
      (min Z b)
      ==.
      -- (min Z ?y) =>
      Z
      ==.
      -- <= (min ?x Z)
      (min b Z)
      ==.
      -- <= prop_32:a=Z
      (min b a)
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_33: (eq (min a b) a) = (leq a b)
prop_33 = VALID (0.01 sec)
{-@prop_33::b: Nat->a: Nat->{ (eq (min a b) a) = (leq a b) }@-}
prop_33::Nat->Nat->Proof
prop_33 b a=
  case a of
    (S a_50) ->
      case b of
        (S b_70) ->
          -- 
          (eq (min a b) a)
          ==.
          -- prop_33:a=(S a_50) =>
          (eq (min (S a_50) b) a)
          ==.
          -- prop_33:a=(S a_50):b=(S b_70) =>
          (eq (min (S a_50) (S b_70)) a)
          ==.
          -- (min (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
          (eq (S (min a_50 b_70)) a)
          ==.
          -- prop_33:a=(S a_50) =>
          (eq (S (min a_50 b_70)) (S a_50))
          ==.
          -- (eq (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
          (eq (min a_50 b_70) a_50)
          ==.
          -- <= lemma-(leq ?a ?b)=(eq (min ?a ?b) ?a)
          (leq a_50 b_70)
          ==.
          -- <= (leq (S ?x) (S ?y))
          (leq (S a_50) (S b_70))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_33:a=(S a_50)
          (leq a (S b_70))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_33:a=(S a_50):b=(S b_70)
          (leq a b)
          ***
          QED
        (Z ) ->
          -- 
          (eq (min a b) a)
          ==.
          -- prop_33:a=(S a_50):b=Z =>
          (eq (min a Z) a)
          ==.
          -- (min ?x Z) =>
          (eq Z a)
          ==.
          -- prop_33:a=(S a_50) =>
          (eq Z (S a_50))
          ==.
          -- (eq Z (S ?y)) =>
          False
          ==.
          -- <= (leq (S ?x) Z)
          (leq (S a_50) Z)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_33:a=(S a_50)
          (leq a Z)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_33:a=(S a_50):b=Z
          (leq a b)
          ***
          QED
    (Z ) ->
      -- 
      (eq (min a b) a)
      ==.
      -- prop_33:a=Z =>
      (eq (min Z b) a)
      ==.
      -- (min Z ?y) =>
      (eq Z a)
      ==.
      -- prop_33:a=Z =>
      (eq Z Z)
      ==.
      -- (eq Z Z) =>
      True
      ==.
      -- <= (leq Z ?y)
      (leq Z b)
      ==.
      -- <= prop_33:a=Z
      (leq a b)
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_35: (dropWhile ($ const False) xs) = xs
prop_35 = VALID (0.01 sec)
{-@prop_35::xs: (List a)->{ (dropWhile ($ const False) xs) = xs }@-}
prop_35::(List a)->Proof
prop_35 xs=
  case xs of
    (Cons xs_50 xs_51) ->
      -- 
      (dropWhile (($) const False) xs)
      ==.
      -- prop_35:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51) =>
      (dropWhile (($) const False) (Cons xs_50 xs_51))
      ==.
      -- (dropWhile ?p (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
      (ite (($) (($) const False) xs_50) (dropWhile (($) const False) xs_51) (Cons xs_50 xs_51))
      ==.
      -- <= prop_35:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51)
      (ite (($) (($) const False) xs_50) (dropWhile (($) const False) xs_51) xs)
      ==.
      -- apply-const =>
      (ite (const False xs_50) (dropWhile (($) const False) xs_51) xs)
      ==.
      -- (const ?x ?y) =>
      (ite False (dropWhile (($) const False) xs_51) xs)
      ==.
      -- <= lemma-?xs=(dropWhile ($ const False) ?xs)
      (ite False xs_51 xs)
      ==.
      -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
      xs
      ***
      QED
    (Nil ) ->
      -- 
      (dropWhile (($) const False) xs)
      ==.
      -- prop_35:xs=Nil =>
      (dropWhile (($) const False) Nil)
      ==.
      -- (dropWhile ?p Nil) =>
      Nil
      ==.
      -- <= prop_35:xs=Nil
      xs
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_36: (takeWhile ($ const True) xs) = xs
prop_36 = VALID (0.01 sec)
{-@prop_36::xs: (List a)->{ (takeWhile ($ const True) xs) = xs }@-}
prop_36::(List a)->Proof
prop_36 xs=
  case xs of
    (Cons xs_50 xs_51) ->
      -- 
      (takeWhile (($) const True) xs)
      ==.
      -- prop_36:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51) =>
      (takeWhile (($) const True) (Cons xs_50 xs_51))
      ==.
      -- (takeWhile ?p (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
      (ite (($) (($) const True) xs_50) (Cons xs_50 (takeWhile (($) const True) xs_51)) Nil)
      ==.
      -- apply-const =>
      (ite (const True xs_50) (Cons xs_50 (takeWhile (($) const True) xs_51)) Nil)
      ==.
      -- (const ?x ?y) =>
      (ite True (Cons xs_50 (takeWhile (($) const True) xs_51)) Nil)
      ==.
      -- <= lemma-?xs=(takeWhile ($ const True) ?xs)
      (ite True (Cons xs_50 xs_51) Nil)
      ==.
      -- <= prop_36:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51)
      (ite True xs Nil)
      ==.
      -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
      xs
      ***
      QED
    (Nil ) ->
      -- 
      (takeWhile (($) const True) xs)
      ==.
      -- prop_36:xs=Nil =>
      (takeWhile (($) const True) Nil)
      ==.
      -- (takeWhile ?p Nil) =>
      Nil
      ==.
      -- <= prop_36:xs=Nil
      xs
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_37: (not (elem x (delete x xs))) = True
prop_37 = INVALID (0.06 sec)
Proving begin prop_38: (count n (append xs (Cons n Nil))) = (S (count n xs))
prop_38 = VALID (0.13 sec)
{-@prop_38::xs: (List Nat)->n: Nat->{ (count n (append xs (Cons n Nil))) = (S (count n xs)) }@-}
prop_38::(List Nat)->Nat->Proof
prop_38 xs n=
  case n of
    (S n_80) ->
      case xs of
        (Cons xs_100 xs_101) ->
          case g-13 of
            (False ) ->
              -- 
              (count n (append xs (Cons n Nil)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101) =>
              (count n (append (Cons xs_100 xs_101) (Cons n Nil)))
              ==.
              -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
              (count n (Cons xs_100 (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
              (ite (eq n xs_100) (S (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil)))) (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (ite g-13 (S (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil)))) (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101):g-13=False =>
              (ite False (S (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil)))) (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
              (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=(S n_80) =>
              (count (S n_80) (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=(S n_80) =>
              (count (S n_80) (append xs_101 (Cons (S n_80) Nil)))
              ==.
              -- <= lemma-(S (count (S ?n_80) ?xs))=(count (S ?n_80) (append ?xs (Cons (S ?n_80) Nil)))
              (S (count (S n_80) xs_101))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_38:n=(S n_80)
              (S (count n xs_101))
              ==.
              -- <= (ite False ?x ?y)
              (S (ite False (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))) (count n xs_101)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101):g-13=False
              (S (ite g-13 (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))) (count n xs_101)))
              ==.
              -- <= add guard scrutinee
              (S (ite (eq n xs_100) (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))) (count n xs_101)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=(S n_80) =>
              (S (ite (eq n xs_100) (count (S n_80) (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))) (count n xs_101)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=(S n_80) =>
              (S (ite (eq n xs_100) (count (S n_80) (append xs_101 (Cons (S n_80) Nil))) (count n xs_101)))
              ==.
              -- <= lemma-(S (count (S ?n_80) ?xs))=(count (S ?n_80) (append ?xs (Cons (S ?n_80) Nil)))
              (S (ite (eq n xs_100) (S (count (S n_80) xs_101)) (count n xs_101)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_38:n=(S n_80)
              (S (ite (eq n xs_100) (S (count n xs_101)) (count n xs_101)))
              ==.
              -- <= (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))
              (S (count n (Cons xs_100 xs_101)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101)
              (S (count n xs))
              ***
              QED
            (True ) ->
              -- 
              (count n (append xs (Cons n Nil)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101) =>
              (count n (append (Cons xs_100 xs_101) (Cons n Nil)))
              ==.
              -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
              (count n (Cons xs_100 (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
              (ite (eq n xs_100) (S (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil)))) (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (ite g-13 (S (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil)))) (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101):g-13=True =>
              (ite True (S (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil)))) (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
              (S (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- <= (ite True ?x ?y)
              (S (ite True (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))) (count n xs_101)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101):g-13=True
              (S (ite g-13 (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))) (count n xs_101)))
              ==.
              -- <= add guard scrutinee
              (S (ite (eq n xs_100) (count n (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))) (count n xs_101)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=(S n_80) =>
              (S (ite (eq n xs_100) (count (S n_80) (append xs_101 (Cons n Nil))) (count n xs_101)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=(S n_80) =>
              (S (ite (eq n xs_100) (count (S n_80) (append xs_101 (Cons (S n_80) Nil))) (count n xs_101)))
              ==.
              -- <= lemma-(S (count (S ?n_80) ?xs))=(count (S ?n_80) (append ?xs (Cons (S ?n_80) Nil)))
              (S (ite (eq n xs_100) (S (count (S n_80) xs_101)) (count n xs_101)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_38:n=(S n_80)
              (S (ite (eq n xs_100) (S (count n xs_101)) (count n xs_101)))
              ==.
              -- <= (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))
              (S (count n (Cons xs_100 xs_101)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=(Cons xs_100 xs_101)
              (S (count n xs))
              ***
              QED
        (Nil ) ->
          case g-13 of
            (False ) ->
              case n_80 of
                (S n_80_180) ->
                  -- 
                  (count n (append xs (Cons n Nil)))
                  ==.
                  -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil =>
                  (count n (append Nil (Cons n Nil)))
                  ==.
                  -- (append Nil ?ys) =>
                  (count n (Cons n Nil))
                  ==.
                  -- <= prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil
                  (count n (Cons n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
                  (ite (eq n n) (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- prop_38:n=(S n_80) =>
                  (ite (eq (S n_80) n) (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- prop_38:n=(S n_80) =>
                  (ite (eq (S n_80) (S n_80)) (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- (eq (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
                  (ite (eq n_80 n_80) (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil:g-13=False:n_80=(S n_80_180) =>
                  (ite (eq (S n_80_180) n_80) (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil:g-13=False:n_80=(S n_80_180) =>
                  (ite (eq (S n_80_180) (S n_80_180)) (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil =>
                  (ite (eq (S n_80_180) (S n_80_180)) (S (count n Nil)) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- (count ?x Nil) =>
                  (ite (eq (S n_80_180) (S n_80_180)) (S Z) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil =>
                  (ite (eq (S n_80_180) (S n_80_180)) (S Z) (count n Nil))
                  ==.
                  -- (count ?x Nil) =>
                  (ite (eq (S n_80_180) (S n_80_180)) (S Z) Z)
                  ==.
                  -- lemma-(ite (eq (S ?n_80) (S ?n_80)) (S Z) Z)=(S Z) =>
                  (S Z)
                  ==.
                  -- <= (count ?x Nil)
                  (S (count n Nil))
                  ==.
                  -- <= prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil
                  (S (count n xs))
                  ***
                  QED
                (Z ) ->
                  -- 
                  (count n (append xs (Cons n Nil)))
                  ==.
                  -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil =>
                  (count n (append Nil (Cons n Nil)))
                  ==.
                  -- (append Nil ?ys) =>
                  (count n (Cons n Nil))
                  ==.
                  -- <= prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil
                  (count n (Cons n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
                  (ite (eq n n) (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- prop_38:n=(S n_80) =>
                  (ite (eq (S n_80) n) (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- prop_38:n=(S n_80) =>
                  (ite (eq (S n_80) (S n_80)) (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- (eq (S ?x) (S ?y)) =>
                  (ite (eq n_80 n_80) (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil:g-13=False:n_80=Z =>
                  (ite (eq Z n_80) (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil:g-13=False:n_80=Z =>
                  (ite (eq Z Z) (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- (eq Z Z) =>
                  (ite True (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil =>
                  (ite True (S (count n Nil)) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- (count ?x Nil) =>
                  (ite True (S Z) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- <= prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil:g-13=False:n_80=Z
                  (ite True (S n_80) (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- <= prop_38:n=(S n_80)
                  (ite True n (count n xs))
                  ==.
                  -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil =>
                  (ite True n (count n Nil))
                  ==.
                  -- (count ?x Nil) =>
                  (ite True n Z)
                  ==.

                  (ite True n n_80)
                  ==.
                  -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
                  n
                  ==.

                  (S n_80)
                  ==.
                  -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil:g-13=False:n_80=Z =>
                  (S Z)
                  ==.
                  -- <= (count ?x Nil)
                  (S (count n Nil))
                  ==.
                  -- <= prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil
                  (S (count n xs))
                  ***
                  QED
            (True ) ->
              -- 
              (count n (append xs (Cons n Nil)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil =>
              (count n (append Nil (Cons n Nil)))
              ==.
              -- (append Nil ?ys) =>
              (count n (Cons n Nil))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil
              (count n (Cons n xs))
              ==.
              -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
              (ite (eq n n) (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (ite g-13 (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=(S n_80):xs=Nil:g-13=True =>
              (ite True (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
              ==.
              -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
              (S (count n xs))
              ***
              QED
    (Z ) ->
      case xs of
        (Cons xs_90 xs_91) ->
          case g-12 of
            (False ) ->
              -- 
              (count n (append xs (Cons n Nil)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91) =>
              (count n (append (Cons xs_90 xs_91) (Cons n Nil)))
              ==.
              -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
              (count n (Cons xs_90 (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
              (ite (eq n xs_90) (S (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil)))) (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (ite g-12 (S (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil)))) (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91):g-12=False =>
              (ite False (S (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil)))) (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
              (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=Z =>
              (count Z (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=Z =>
              (count Z (append xs_91 (Cons Z Nil)))
              ==.
              -- <= lemma-(S (count Z ?xs))=(count Z (append ?xs (Cons Z Nil)))
              (S (count Z xs_91))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_38:n=Z
              (S (count n xs_91))
              ==.
              -- <= (ite False ?x ?y)
              (S (ite False (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))) (count n xs_91)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_38:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91):g-12=False
              (S (ite g-12 (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))) (count n xs_91)))
              ==.
              -- <= add guard scrutinee
              (S (ite (eq n xs_90) (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))) (count n xs_91)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=Z =>
              (S (ite (eq n xs_90) (count Z (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))) (count n xs_91)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=Z =>
              (S (ite (eq n xs_90) (count Z (append xs_91 (Cons Z Nil))) (count n xs_91)))
              ==.
              -- <= lemma-(S (count Z ?xs))=(count Z (append ?xs (Cons Z Nil)))
              (S (ite (eq n xs_90) (S (count Z xs_91)) (count n xs_91)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_38:n=Z
              (S (ite (eq n xs_90) (S (count n xs_91)) (count n xs_91)))
              ==.
              -- <= (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))
              (S (count n (Cons xs_90 xs_91)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_38:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91)
              (S (count n xs))
              ***
              QED
            (True ) ->
              -- 
              (count n (append xs (Cons n Nil)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91) =>
              (count n (append (Cons xs_90 xs_91) (Cons n Nil)))
              ==.
              -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
              (count n (Cons xs_90 (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
              (ite (eq n xs_90) (S (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil)))) (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- add guard scrutinee =>
              (ite g-12 (S (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil)))) (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91):g-12=True =>
              (ite True (S (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil)))) (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
              (S (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))))
              ==.
              -- <= (ite True ?x ?y)
              (S (ite True (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))) (count n xs_91)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_38:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91):g-12=True
              (S (ite g-12 (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))) (count n xs_91)))
              ==.
              -- <= add guard scrutinee
              (S (ite (eq n xs_90) (count n (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))) (count n xs_91)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=Z =>
              (S (ite (eq n xs_90) (count Z (append xs_91 (Cons n Nil))) (count n xs_91)))
              ==.
              -- prop_38:n=Z =>
              (S (ite (eq n xs_90) (count Z (append xs_91 (Cons Z Nil))) (count n xs_91)))
              ==.
              -- <= lemma-(S (count Z ?xs))=(count Z (append ?xs (Cons Z Nil)))
              (S (ite (eq n xs_90) (S (count Z xs_91)) (count n xs_91)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_38:n=Z
              (S (ite (eq n xs_90) (S (count n xs_91)) (count n xs_91)))
              ==.
              -- <= (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))
              (S (count n (Cons xs_90 xs_91)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_38:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91)
              (S (count n xs))
              ***
              QED
        (Nil ) ->
          -- 
          (count n (append xs (Cons n Nil)))
          ==.
          -- prop_38:n=Z:xs=Nil =>
          (count n (append Nil (Cons n Nil)))
          ==.
          -- (append Nil ?ys) =>
          (count n (Cons n Nil))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_38:n=Z:xs=Nil
          (count n (Cons n xs))
          ==.
          -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
          (ite (eq n n) (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
          ==.

          (ite (eq n n) (S (count n xs)) (count n Nil))
          ==.
          -- (count ?x Nil) =>
          (ite (eq n n) (S (count n xs)) Z)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_38:n=Z
          (ite (eq n n) (S (count n xs)) n)
          ==.
          -- prop_38:n=Z =>
          (ite (eq Z n) (S (count n xs)) n)
          ==.
          -- prop_38:n=Z =>
          (ite (eq Z Z) (S (count n xs)) n)
          ==.
          -- (eq Z Z) =>
          (ite True (S (count n xs)) n)
          ==.
          -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
          (S (count n xs))
          ***
          QED

Proving begin prop_39: (add (count n (Cons x Nil)) (count n xs)) = (count n (Cons x xs))
prop_39 = VALID (0.03 sec)
{-@prop_39::x: Nat->xs: (List Nat)->n: Nat->{ (add (count n (Cons x Nil)) (count n xs)) = (count n (Cons x xs)) }@-}
prop_39::Nat->(List Nat)->Nat->Proof
prop_39 x xs n=
  case g-10 of
    (False ) ->
      -- 
      (add (count n (Cons x Nil)) (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
      (add (ite (eq n x) (S (count n Nil)) (count n Nil)) (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- add guard scrutinee =>
      (add (ite g-10 (S (count n Nil)) (count n Nil)) (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- prop_39:g-10=False =>
      (add (ite False (S (count n Nil)) (count n Nil)) (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
      (add (count n Nil) (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- (count ?x Nil) =>
      (add Z (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- (add Z ?y) =>
      (count n xs)
      ==.
      -- <= (ite False ?x ?y)
      (ite False (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- <= prop_39:g-10=False
      (ite g-10 (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- <= add guard scrutinee
      (ite (eq n x) (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- <= (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))
      (count n (Cons x xs))
      ***
      QED
    (True ) ->
      -- 
      (add (count n (Cons x Nil)) (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
      (add (ite (eq n x) (S (count n Nil)) (count n Nil)) (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- add guard scrutinee =>
      (add (ite g-10 (S (count n Nil)) (count n Nil)) (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- prop_39:g-10=True =>
      (add (ite True (S (count n Nil)) (count n Nil)) (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
      (add (S (count n Nil)) (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- (add (S ?x) ?y) =>
      (S (add (count n Nil) (count n xs)))
      ==.
      -- (count ?x Nil) =>
      (S (add Z (count n xs)))
      ==.
      -- (add Z ?y) =>
      (S (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- <= (ite True ?x ?y)
      (ite True (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- <= prop_39:g-10=True
      (ite g-10 (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- <= add guard scrutinee
      (ite (eq n x) (S (count n xs)) (count n xs))
      ==.
      -- <= (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))
      (count n (Cons x xs))
      ***
      QED
