Proving begin prop_41: (take n (map f xs)) = (map f (take n xs))
prop_41 = VALID (0.01 sec)
{-@prop_41::f: (-> a b)->n: Nat->xs: (List a)->{ (take n (map f xs)) = (map f (take n xs)) }@-}
prop_41::(-> a b)->Nat->(List a)->Proof
prop_41 f n xs=
  case n of
    (S n_70) ->
      case xs of
        (Cons xs_90 xs_91) ->
          -- 
          (take n (map f xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_41:n=(S n_70) =>
          (take (S n_70) (map f xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_41:n=(S n_70):xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91) =>
          (take (S n_70) (map f (Cons xs_90 xs_91)))
          ==.
          -- (map ?f (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
          (take (S n_70) (Cons (($) f xs_90) (map f xs_91)))
          ==.
          -- (take (S ?n) (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
          (Cons (($) f xs_90) (take n_70 (map f xs_91)))
          ==.
          -- lemma-(take ?n (map ?f ?xs))=(map ?f (take ?n ?xs)) =>
          (Cons (($) f xs_90) (map f (take n_70 xs_91)))
          ==.
          -- <= (map ?f (Cons ?x ?xs))
          (map f (Cons xs_90 (take n_70 xs_91)))
          ==.
          -- <= (take (S ?n) (Cons ?x ?xs))
          (map f (take (S n_70) (Cons xs_90 xs_91)))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_41:n=(S n_70)
          (map f (take n (Cons xs_90 xs_91)))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_41:n=(S n_70):xs=(Cons xs_90 xs_91)
          (map f (take n xs))
          ***
          QED
        (Nil ) ->
          -- 
          (take n (map f xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_41:n=(S n_70):xs=Nil =>
          (take n (map f Nil))
          ==.
          -- (map ?f Nil) =>
          (take n Nil)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_41:n=(S n_70):xs=Nil
          (take n xs)
          ==.
          -- prop_41:n=(S n_70) =>
          (take (S n_70) xs)
          ==.
          -- prop_41:n=(S n_70):xs=Nil =>
          (take (S n_70) Nil)
          ==.
          -- (take (S ?n) Nil) =>
          Nil
          ==.
          -- <= (map ?f Nil)
          (map f Nil)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_41:n=(S n_70):xs=Nil
          (map f xs)
          ==.
          -- prop_41:n=(S n_70):xs=Nil =>
          (map f Nil)
          ==.
          -- <= (take (S ?n) Nil)
          (map f (take (S n_70) Nil))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_41:n=(S n_70)
          (map f (take n Nil))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_41:n=(S n_70):xs=Nil
          (map f (take n xs))
          ***
          QED
    (Z ) ->
      -- 
      (take n (map f xs))
      ==.
      -- prop_41:n=Z =>
      (take Z (map f xs))
      ==.
      -- (take Z ?xs) =>
      Nil
      ==.
      -- <= (map ?f Nil)
      (map f Nil)
      ==.
      -- <= (take Z ?xs)
      (map f (take Z xs))
      ==.
      -- <= prop_41:n=Z
      (map f (take n xs))
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_43: (append (takeWhile p xs) (dropWhile p xs)) = xs
prop_43 = VALID (0.01 sec)
{-@prop_43::xs: (List a)->p: (-> a Bool)->{ (append (takeWhile p xs) (dropWhile p xs)) = xs }@-}
prop_43::(List a)->(-> a Bool)->Proof
prop_43 xs p=
  case xs of
    (Cons xs_50 xs_51) ->
      case g-8 of
        (False ) ->
          -- 
          (append (takeWhile p xs) (dropWhile p xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_43:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51) =>
          (append (takeWhile p (Cons xs_50 xs_51)) (dropWhile p xs))
          ==.
          -- (takeWhile ?p (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
          (append (ite (($) p xs_50) (Cons xs_50 (takeWhile p xs_51)) Nil) (dropWhile p xs))
          ==.
          -- add guard scrutinee =>
          (append (ite g-8 (Cons xs_50 (takeWhile p xs_51)) Nil) (dropWhile p xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_43:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):g-8=False =>
          (append (ite False (Cons xs_50 (takeWhile p xs_51)) Nil) (dropWhile p xs))
          ==.
          -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
          (append Nil (dropWhile p xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_43:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51) =>
          (append Nil (dropWhile p (Cons xs_50 xs_51)))
          ==.
          -- (dropWhile ?p (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
          (append Nil (ite (($) p xs_50) (dropWhile p xs_51) (Cons xs_50 xs_51)))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_43:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51)
          (append Nil (ite (($) p xs_50) (dropWhile p xs_51) xs))
          ==.
          -- add guard scrutinee =>
          (append Nil (ite g-8 (dropWhile p xs_51) xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_43:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):g-8=False =>
          (append Nil (ite False (dropWhile p xs_51) xs))
          ==.
          -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
          (append Nil xs)
          ==.
          -- (append Nil ?ys) =>
          xs
          ***
          QED
        (True ) ->
          -- 
          (append (takeWhile p xs) (dropWhile p xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_43:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51) =>
          (append (takeWhile p (Cons xs_50 xs_51)) (dropWhile p xs))
          ==.
          -- (takeWhile ?p (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
          (append (ite (($) p xs_50) (Cons xs_50 (takeWhile p xs_51)) Nil) (dropWhile p xs))
          ==.
          -- add guard scrutinee =>
          (append (ite g-8 (Cons xs_50 (takeWhile p xs_51)) Nil) (dropWhile p xs))
          ==.
          -- prop_43:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):g-8=True =>
          (append (ite True (Cons xs_50 (takeWhile p xs_51)) Nil) (dropWhile p xs))
          ==.
          -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
          (append (Cons xs_50 (takeWhile p xs_51)) (dropWhile p xs))
          ==.
          -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
          (Cons xs_50 (append (takeWhile p xs_51) (dropWhile p xs)))
          ==.
          -- prop_43:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51) =>
          (Cons xs_50 (append (takeWhile p xs_51) (dropWhile p (Cons xs_50 xs_51))))
          ==.
          -- (dropWhile ?p (Cons ?x ?xs)) =>
          (Cons xs_50 (append (takeWhile p xs_51) (ite (($) p xs_50) (dropWhile p xs_51) (Cons xs_50 xs_51))))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_43:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51)
          (Cons xs_50 (append (takeWhile p xs_51) (ite (($) p xs_50) (dropWhile p xs_51) xs)))
          ==.
          -- add guard scrutinee =>
          (Cons xs_50 (append (takeWhile p xs_51) (ite g-8 (dropWhile p xs_51) xs)))
          ==.
          -- prop_43:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):g-8=True =>
          (Cons xs_50 (append (takeWhile p xs_51) (ite True (dropWhile p xs_51) xs)))
          ==.
          -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
          (Cons xs_50 (append (takeWhile p xs_51) (dropWhile p xs_51)))
          ==.
          -- lemma-(append (takeWhile ?p ?xs) (dropWhile ?p ?xs))=?xs =>
          (Cons xs_50 xs_51)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_43:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51)
          xs
          ***
          QED
    (Nil ) ->
      --

      (append Nil Nil)
      ==.
      -- <= prop_43:xs=Nil
      (append Nil xs)
      ==.
      -- (append Nil ?ys) =>
      xs
      ***
      QED

          Nil
          ==.
          -- <= (zipConcat ?x ?xs Nil)
          (zipConcat x xs Nil)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_44:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):ys=Nil
          (zipConcat x xs ys)

    (Nil ) ->
      case ys of

          (zip (Cons x xs) ys)

          (zip (Cons x xs) Nil)

          Nil

          ==.

          (zipConcat x Nil Nil)
          ==.

    (Cons xs_50 xs_51) ->
      case ys of
        (Cons ys_100 ys_101) ->

            (Cons xs_51_170 xs_51_171) ->
              -- 
              (butlast (append xs ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51) =>
              (butlast (append (Cons xs_50 xs_51) ys))
              ==.
              -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 (append xs_51 ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=(Cons ys_100 ys_101):xs_51=(Cons xs_51_170 xs_51_171) =>
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 (append (Cons xs_51_170 xs_51_171) ys)))
              ==.
              -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 (Cons xs_51_170 (append xs_51_171 ys))))
              ==.
              -- (butlast (Cons ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))) =>
              (Cons xs_50 (butlast (Cons xs_51_170 (append xs_51_171 ys))))
              ==.
              -- prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=(Cons ys_100 ys_101) =>
              (Cons xs_50 (butlast (Cons xs_51_170 (append xs_51_171 (Cons ys_100 ys_101)))))
              ==.
              -- <= lemma-(append (Cons ?xs_50 ?xs_51) (butlast (Cons ?ys_100 ?ys_101)))=(butlast (Cons ?xs_50 (append ?xs_51 (Cons ?ys_100 ?ys_101))))
              (Cons xs_50 (append (Cons xs_51_170 xs_51_171) (butlast (Cons ys_100 ys_101))))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=(Cons ys_100 ys_101):xs_51=(Cons xs_51_170 xs_51_171)
              (Cons xs_50 (append xs_51 (butlast (Cons ys_100 ys_101))))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=(Cons ys_100 ys_101)
              (Cons xs_50 (append xs_51 (butlast ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys)
              (append (Cons xs_50 xs_51) (butlast ys))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51)
              (append xs (butlast ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=(Cons ys_100 ys_101) =>
              (append xs (butlast (Cons ys_100 ys_101)))
              ==.
              -- <= (butlastConcat ?xs (Cons ?y ?ys))
              (butlastConcat xs (Cons ys_100 ys_101))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=(Cons ys_100 ys_101)
              (butlastConcat xs ys)
              ***
              QED
            (Nil ) ->
              -- 
              (butlast (append xs ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51) =>
              (butlast (append (Cons xs_50 xs_51) ys))
              ==.
              -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 (append xs_51 ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=(Cons ys_100 ys_101):xs_51=Nil =>
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 (append Nil ys)))
              ==.
              -- (append Nil ?ys) =>
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=(Cons ys_100 ys_101) =>
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 (Cons ys_100 ys_101)))
              ==.
              -- (butlast (Cons ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))) =>
              (Cons xs_50 (butlast (Cons ys_100 ys_101)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=(Cons ys_100 ys_101)
              (Cons xs_50 (butlast ys))
              ==.
              -- <= (append Nil ?ys)
              (Cons xs_50 (append Nil (butlast ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=(Cons ys_100 ys_101):xs_51=Nil
              (Cons xs_50 (append xs_51 (butlast ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys)
              (append (Cons xs_50 xs_51) (butlast ys))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51)
              (append xs (butlast ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=(Cons ys_100 ys_101) =>
              (append xs (butlast (Cons ys_100 ys_101)))
              ==.
              -- <= (butlastConcat ?xs (Cons ?y ?ys))
              (butlastConcat xs (Cons ys_100 ys_101))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=(Cons ys_100 ys_101)
              (butlastConcat xs ys)
              ***
              QED
        (Nil ) ->
          case xs_51 of
            (Cons xs_51_120 xs_51_121) ->
              -- 
              (butlast (append xs ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51) =>
              (butlast (append (Cons xs_50 xs_51) ys))
              ==.
              -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 (append xs_51 ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=Nil:xs_51=(Cons xs_51_120 xs_51_121) =>
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 (append (Cons xs_51_120 xs_51_121) ys)))
              ==.
              -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 (Cons xs_51_120 (append xs_51_121 ys))))
              ==.
              -- (butlast (Cons ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))) =>
              (Cons xs_50 (butlast (Cons xs_51_120 (append xs_51_121 ys))))
              ==.
              -- <= (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys)
              (Cons xs_50 (butlast (append (Cons xs_51_120 xs_51_121) ys)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=Nil:xs_51=(Cons xs_51_120 xs_51_121)
              (Cons xs_50 (butlast (append xs_51 ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=Nil:xs_51=(Cons xs_51_120 xs_51_121) =>
              (Cons xs_50 (butlast (append (Cons xs_51_120 xs_51_121) ys)))
              ==.
              -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
              (Cons xs_50 (butlast (Cons xs_51_120 (append xs_51_121 ys))))
              ==.
              -- prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=Nil =>
              (Cons xs_50 (butlast (Cons xs_51_120 (append xs_51_121 Nil))))
              ==.
              -- <= lemma-(butlast (Cons ?xs_50 ?xs_51))=(butlast (Cons ?xs_50 (append ?xs_51 Nil)))
              (Cons xs_50 (butlast (Cons xs_51_120 xs_51_121)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=Nil:xs_51=(Cons xs_51_120 xs_51_121)
              (Cons xs_50 (butlast xs_51))
              ==.
              -- prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=Nil:xs_51=(Cons xs_51_120 xs_51_121) =>
              (Cons xs_50 (butlast (Cons xs_51_120 xs_51_121)))
              ==.
              -- <= (butlast (Cons ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)))
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 (Cons xs_51_120 xs_51_121)))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=Nil:xs_51=(Cons xs_51_120 xs_51_121)
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 xs_51))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51)
              (butlast xs)
              ==.
              -- <= (butlastConcat ?xs Nil)
              (butlastConcat xs Nil)
              ==.
              -- <= prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=Nil
              (butlastConcat xs ys)
              ***
              QED
            (Nil ) ->
              -- 
              (butlast (append xs ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51) =>
              (butlast (append (Cons xs_50 xs_51) ys))
              ==.
              -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 (append xs_51 ys)))
              ==.
              -- prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=Nil:xs_51=Nil =>
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 (append Nil ys)))
              ==.
              -- (append Nil ?ys) =>
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 ys))
              ==.
              -- prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=Nil =>
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 Nil))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=Nil:xs_51=Nil
              (butlast (Cons xs_50 xs_51))
              ==.
              -- <= prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51)
              (butlast xs)
              ==.
              -- <= (butlastConcat ?xs Nil)
              (butlastConcat xs Nil)
              ==.
              -- <= prop_49:xs=(Cons xs_50 xs_51):ys=Nil
              (butlastConcat xs ys)
              ***
              QED
    (Nil ) ->
      case ys of
        (Cons ys_70 ys_71) ->
          -- 
          (butlast (append xs ys))
          ==.
          -- <= (append Nil ?ys)
          (append Nil (butlast (append xs ys)))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_49:xs=Nil
          (append xs (butlast (append xs ys)))
          ==.
          -- prop_49:xs=Nil =>
          (append xs (butlast (append Nil ys)))
          ==.
          -- (append Nil ?ys) =>
          (append xs (butlast ys))
          ==.
          -- prop_49:xs=Nil:ys=(Cons ys_70 ys_71) =>
          (append xs (butlast (Cons ys_70 ys_71)))
          ==.
          -- <= (butlastConcat ?xs (Cons ?y ?ys))
          (butlastConcat xs (Cons ys_70 ys_71))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_49:xs=Nil:ys=(Cons ys_70 ys_71)
          (butlastConcat xs ys)
          ***
          QED
        (Nil ) ->
          -- 
          (butlast (append xs ys))
          ==.
          -- prop_49:xs=Nil =>
          (butlast (append Nil ys))
          ==.
          -- (append Nil ?ys) =>
          (butlast ys)
          ==.
          -- <= (butlastConcat ?xs Nil)
          (butlastConcat ys Nil)
          ==.
          -- prop_49:xs=Nil:ys=Nil =>
          (butlastConcat Nil Nil)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_49:xs=Nil
          (butlastConcat xs Nil)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_49:xs=Nil:ys=Nil
          (butlastConcat xs ys)
          ***
          QED

Proving begin prop_50: (butlast xs) = (take (sub (len xs) (S Z)) xs)
prop_50 = VALID (0.02 sec)
{-@prop_50::xs: (List a)->{ (butlast xs) = (take (sub (len xs) (S Z)) xs) }@-}
prop_50::(List a)->Proof
prop_50 xs=
  case xs of
    (Cons xs_70 xs_71) ->
      case xs_71 of
        (Cons xs_71_140 xs_71_141) ->
          -- 
          (butlast xs)
          ==.
          -- prop_50:xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71) =>
          (butlast (Cons xs_70 xs_71))
          ==.
          -- prop_50:xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71):xs_71=(Cons xs_71_140 xs_71_141) =>
          (butlast (Cons xs_70 (Cons xs_71_140 xs_71_141)))
          ==.
          -- (butlast (Cons ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))) =>
          (Cons xs_70 (butlast (Cons xs_71_140 xs_71_141)))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_50:xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71):xs_71=(Cons xs_71_140 xs_71_141)
          (Cons xs_70 (butlast xs_71))
          ==.
          -- prop_50:xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71):xs_71=(Cons xs_71_140 xs_71_141) =>
          (Cons xs_70 (butlast (Cons xs_71_140 xs_71_141)))
          ==.
          -- lemma-(butlast (Cons ?xs_70 ?xs_71))=(take (len ?xs_71) (Cons ?xs_70 ?xs_71)) =>
          (Cons xs_70 (take (len xs_71_141) (Cons xs_71_140 xs_71_141)))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_50:xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71):xs_71=(Cons xs_71_140 xs_71_141)
          (Cons xs_70 (take (len xs_71_141) xs_71))
          ==.
          -- <= (take (S ?n) (Cons ?x ?xs))
          (take (S (len xs_71_141)) (Cons xs_70 xs_71))
          ==.
          -- <= (len (Cons ?x ?xs))
          (take (len (Cons xs_71_140 xs_71_141)) (Cons xs_70 xs_71))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_50:xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71):xs_71=(Cons xs_71_140 xs_71_141)
          (take (len xs_71) (Cons xs_70 xs_71))
          ==.
          -- <= (sub ?x Z)
          (take (sub (len xs_71) Z) (Cons xs_70 xs_71))
          ==.
          -- <= (sub (S ?x) (S ?y))
          (take (sub (S (len xs_71)) (S Z)) (Cons xs_70 xs_71))
          ==.
          -- <= (len (Cons ?x ?xs))
          (take (sub (len (Cons xs_70 xs_71)) (S Z)) (Cons xs_70 xs_71))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_50:xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71)
          (take (sub (len xs) (S Z)) (Cons xs_70 xs_71))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_50:xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71)
          (take (sub (len xs) (S Z)) xs)
          ***
          QED
        (Nil ) ->
          -- 
          (butlast xs)
          ==.
          -- prop_50:xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71) =>
          (butlast (Cons xs_70 xs_71))
          ==.
          -- prop_50:xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71):xs_71=Nil =>
          (butlast (Cons xs_70 Nil))
          ==.
          -- (butlast (Cons ?x Nil)) =>
          Nil
          ==.
          -- <= (take Z ?xs)
          (take Z xs)
          ==.
          -- <= (len Nil)
          (take (len Nil) xs)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_50:xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71):xs_71=Nil
          (take (len xs_71) xs)
          ==.
          -- <= (sub ?x Z)
          (take (sub (len xs_71) Z) xs)
          ==.
          -- <= (sub (S ?x) (S ?y))
          (take (sub (S (len xs_71)) (S Z)) xs)
          ==.
          -- <= (len (Cons ?x ?xs))
          (take (sub (len (Cons xs_70 xs_71)) (S Z)) xs)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_50:xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71)
          (take (sub (len xs) (S Z)) xs)
          ***
          QED
    (Nil ) ->
      -- 
      (butlast xs)
      ==.
      -- prop_50:xs=Nil =>
      (butlast Nil)
      ==.
      -- (butlast Nil) =>
      Nil
      ==.
      -- <= (take Z ?xs)
      (take Z xs)
      ==.
      -- <= (sub Z ?y)
      (take (sub Z (S Z)) xs)
      ==.
      -- <= (len Nil)
      (take (sub (len Nil) (S Z)) xs)
      ==.
      -- <= prop_50:xs=Nil
      (take (sub (len xs) (S Z)) xs)
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_51: (butlast (append xs (Cons x Nil))) = xs
prop_51 = VALID (0.01 sec)
{-@prop_51::x: a->xs: (List a)->{ (butlast (append xs (Cons x Nil))) = xs }@-}
prop_51::a->(List a)->Proof
prop_51 x xs=
  case xs of
    (Cons xs_60 xs_61) ->
      case xs_61 of
        (Cons xs_61_110 xs_61_111) ->
          -- 
          (butlast (append xs (Cons x Nil)))
          ==.
          -- prop_51:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61) =>
          (butlast (append (Cons xs_60 xs_61) (Cons x Nil)))
          ==.
          -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
          (butlast (Cons xs_60 (append xs_61 (Cons x Nil))))
          ==.
          -- prop_51:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):xs_61=(Cons xs_61_110 xs_61_111) =>
          (butlast (Cons xs_60 (append (Cons xs_61_110 xs_61_111) (Cons x Nil))))
          ==.
          -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
          (butlast (Cons xs_60 (Cons xs_61_110 (append xs_61_111 (Cons x Nil)))))
          ==.
          -- (butlast (Cons ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))) =>
          (Cons xs_60 (butlast (Cons xs_61_110 (append xs_61_111 (Cons x Nil)))))
          ==.
          -- <= (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys)
          (Cons xs_60 (butlast (append (Cons xs_61_110 xs_61_111) (Cons x Nil))))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_51:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):xs_61=(Cons xs_61_110 xs_61_111)
          (Cons xs_60 (butlast (append xs_61 (Cons x Nil))))
          ==.
          -- prop_51:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):xs_61=(Cons xs_61_110 xs_61_111) =>
          (Cons xs_60 (butlast (append (Cons xs_61_110 xs_61_111) (Cons x Nil))))
          ==.
          -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
          (Cons xs_60 (butlast (Cons xs_61_110 (append xs_61_111 (Cons x Nil)))))
          ==.
          -- lemma-(butlast (Cons ?xs_60 (append ?xs_61 (Cons ?x Nil))))=(Cons ?xs_60 ?xs_61) =>
          (Cons xs_60 (Cons xs_61_110 xs_61_111))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_51:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):xs_61=(Cons xs_61_110 xs_61_111)
          (Cons xs_60 xs_61)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_51:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61)
          xs
          ***
          QED
        (Nil ) ->
          -- 
          (butlast (append xs (Cons x Nil)))
          ==.
          -- prop_51:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61) =>
          (butlast (append (Cons xs_60 xs_61) (Cons x Nil)))
          ==.
          -- (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys) =>
          (butlast (Cons xs_60 (append xs_61 (Cons x Nil))))
          ==.
          -- prop_51:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):xs_61=Nil =>
          (butlast (Cons xs_60 (append Nil (Cons x Nil))))
          ==.
          -- (append Nil ?ys) =>
          (butlast (Cons xs_60 (Cons x Nil)))
          ==.
          -- <= prop_51:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):xs_61=Nil
          (butlast (Cons xs_60 (Cons x xs_61)))
          ==.
          -- (butlast (Cons ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))) =>
          (Cons xs_60 (butlast (Cons x xs_61)))
          ==.
          -- prop_51:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):xs_61=Nil =>
          (Cons xs_60 (butlast (Cons x Nil)))
          ==.
          -- (butlast (Cons ?x Nil)) =>
          (Cons xs_60 Nil)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_51:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):xs_61=Nil
          (Cons xs_60 xs_61)
          ==.
          -- <= prop_51:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61)
          xs
          ***
          QED
    (Nil ) ->
      -- 
      (butlast (append xs (Cons x Nil)))
      ==.
      -- prop_51:xs=Nil =>
      (butlast (append Nil (Cons x Nil)))
      ==.
      -- (append Nil ?ys) =>
      (butlast (Cons x Nil))
      ==.
      -- (butlast (Cons ?x Nil)) =>
      Nil
      ==.
      -- <= prop_51:xs=Nil
      xs
      ***
      QED

Proving begin prop_52: (count n xs) = (count n (rev xs))
prop_52 = VALID (4.81 sec)
{-@prop_52::n: Nat->xs: (List Nat)->{ (count n xs) = (count n (rev xs)) }@-}
prop_52::Nat->(List Nat)->Proof
prop_52 n xs=
  case n of
    (S n_50) ->
      case xs of
        (Cons xs_70 xs_71) ->
          case g-14 of
            (False ) ->
              case n_50 of
                (S n_50_210) ->
                  case xs_70 of
                    (S xs_70_230) ->
                      case xs_71 of
                        (Cons xs_71_260 xs_71_261) ->
                          -- 
                          (count n xs)
                          ==.
                          -- prop_52:n=(S n_50):xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71) =>
                          (count n (Cons xs_70 xs_71))
                          ==.
                          -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
                          (ite (eq n xs_70) (S (count n xs_71)) (count n xs_71))
                          ==.
                          -- add guard scrutinee =>
                          (ite g-14 (S (count n xs_71)) (count n xs_71))
                          ==.
                          -- prop_52:n=(S n_50):xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71):g-14=False =>
                          (ite False (S (count n xs_71)) (count n xs_71))
                          ==.
                          -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
                          (count n xs_71)
                          ==.
                          -- prop_52:n=(S n_50):xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71):g-14=False:n_50=(S n_50_210):xs_70=(S xs_70_230):xs_71=(Cons xs_71_260 xs_71_261) =>
                          (count n (Cons xs_71_260 xs_71_261))
                          ==.
                          -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
                          (ite (eq n xs_71_260) (S (count n xs_71_261)) (count n xs_71_261))
                          ==.
                          -- prop_52:n=(S n_50) =>
                          (ite (eq n xs_71_260) (S (count (S n_50) xs_71_261)) (count n xs_71_261))
                          ==.
                          -- prop_52:n=(S n_50):xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71):g-14=False:n_50=(S n_50_210) =>
                          (ite (eq n xs_71_260) (S (count (S (S n_50_210)) xs_71_261)) (count n xs_71_261))
                          ==.
                          -- <= lemma-(count (S (S ?n_50_210)) (append ?xs_71 (Cons (S ?xs_70_230) Nil)))=(count (S (S ?n_50_210)) ?xs_71)
                          (ite (eq n xs_71_260) (S (count (S (S n_50_210)) (append xs_71_261 (Cons (S xs_70_230) Nil)))) (count n xs_71_261))
                          ==.
                          -- <= prop_52:n=(S n_50):xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71):g-14=False:n_50=(S n_50_210)
                          (ite (eq n xs_71_260) (S (count (S n_50) (append xs_71_261 (Cons (S xs_70_230) Nil)))) (count n xs_71_261))
                          ==.
                          -- <= prop_52:n=(S n_50)
                          (ite (eq n xs_71_260) (S (count n (append xs_71_261 (Cons (S xs_70_230) Nil)))) (count n xs_71_261))
                          ==.
                          -- <= prop_52:n=(S n_50):xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71):g-14=False:n_50=(S n_50_210):xs_70=(S xs_70_230)
                          (ite (eq n xs_71_260) (S (count n (append xs_71_261 (Cons xs_70 Nil)))) (count n xs_71_261))
                          ==.
                          -- prop_52:n=(S n_50) =>
                          (ite (eq n xs_71_260) (S (count n (append xs_71_261 (Cons xs_70 Nil)))) (count (S n_50) xs_71_261))
                          ==.
                          -- prop_52:n=(S n_50):xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71):g-14=False:n_50=(S n_50_210) =>
                          (ite (eq n xs_71_260) (S (count n (append xs_71_261 (Cons xs_70 Nil)))) (count (S (S n_50_210)) xs_71_261))
                          ==.
                          -- <= lemma-(count (S (S ?n_50_210)) (append ?xs_71 (Cons (S ?xs_70_230) Nil)))=(count (S (S ?n_50_210)) ?xs_71)
                          (ite (eq n xs_71_260) (S (count n (append xs_71_261 (Cons xs_70 Nil)))) (count (S (S n_50_210)) (append xs_71_261 (Cons (S xs_70_230) Nil))))
                          ==.
                          -- <= prop_52:n=(S n_50):xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71):g-14=False:n_50=(S n_50_210)
                          (ite (eq n xs_71_260) (S (count n (append xs_71_261 (Cons xs_70 Nil)))) (count (S n_50) (append xs_71_261 (Cons (S xs_70_230) Nil))))
                          ==.
                          -- <= prop_52:n=(S n_50)
                          (ite (eq n xs_71_260) (S (count n (append xs_71_261 (Cons xs_70 Nil)))) (count n (append xs_71_261 (Cons (S xs_70_230) Nil))))
                          ==.
                          -- <= prop_52:n=(S n_50):xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71):g-14=False:n_50=(S n_50_210):xs_70=(S xs_70_230)
                          (ite (eq n xs_71_260) (S (count n (append xs_71_261 (Cons xs_70 Nil)))) (count n (append xs_71_261 (Cons xs_70 Nil))))
                          ==.
                          -- <= (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))
                          (count n (Cons xs_71_260 (append xs_71_261 (Cons xs_70 Nil))))
                          ==.
                          -- <= (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys)
                          (count n (append (Cons xs_71_260 xs_71_261) (Cons xs_70 Nil)))
                          ==.
                          -- <= prop_52:n=(S n_50):xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71):g-14=False:n_50=(S n_50_210):xs_70=(S xs_70_230):xs_71=(Cons xs_71_260 xs_71_261)
                          (count n (append xs_71 (Cons xs_70 Nil)))
                          ==.
                          -- <= (rev (Cons ?x ?xs))
                          (count n (rev (Cons xs_70 xs_71)))
                          ==.
                          -- <= prop_52:n=(S n_50):xs=(Cons xs_70 xs_71)
                          (count n (rev xs))
                          ***
                          QED
                        (Nil ) ->
                          -- 
                          (count n xs)
                          ==.
                          -- <= (append Nil ?ys)
                          (count n (append Nil xs))
                          ==.

                      -- <= prop_52:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):g-13=True:xs_60=(S xs_60_200):xs_61=(Cons xs_61_240 xs_61_241)
                      (count n (append xs_61 (Cons xs_60 Nil)))
                      ==.
                      -- <= (rev (Cons ?x ?xs))
                      (count n (rev (Cons xs_60 xs_61)))
                      ==.
                      -- <= prop_52:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61)
                      (count n (rev xs))
                      ***
                      QED
                    (Nil ) ->
                      -- 
                      (count n xs)
                      ==.
                      -- <= (append Nil ?ys)
                      (count n (append Nil xs))
                      ==.
                      -- <= prop_52:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):g-13=True:xs_60=(S xs_60_200):xs_61=Nil
                      (count n (append xs_61 xs))
                      ==.
                      -- prop_52:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61) =>
                      (count n (append xs_61 (Cons xs_60 xs_61)))
                      ==.
                      -- prop_52:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):g-13=True:xs_60=(S xs_60_200):xs_61=Nil =>
                      (count n (append xs_61 (Cons xs_60 Nil)))
                      ==.
                      -- <= (rev (Cons ?x ?xs))
                      (count n (rev (Cons xs_60 xs_61)))
                      ==.
                      -- <= prop_52:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61)
                      (count n (rev xs))
                      ***
                      QED
                (Z ) ->
                  case xs_61 of
                    (Cons xs_61_230 xs_61_231) ->
                      case g-34 of
                        (False ) ->
                          -- 
                          (count n xs)
                          ==.
                          -- prop_52:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61) =>
                          (count n (Cons xs_60 xs_61))
                          ==.
                          -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
                          (ite (eq n xs_60) (S (count n xs_61)) (count n xs_61))
                          ==.
                          -- add guard scrutinee =>
                          (ite g-13 (S (count n xs_61)) (count n xs_61))
                          ==.
                          -- prop_52:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):g-13=True =>
                          (ite True (S (count n xs_61)) (count n xs_61))
                          ==.
                          -- (ite True ?x ?y) =>
                          (S (count n xs_61))
                          ==.
                          -- prop_52:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):g-13=True:xs_60=Z:xs_61=(Cons xs_61_230 xs_61_231) =>
                          (S (count n (Cons xs_61_230 xs_61_231)))
                          ==.
                          -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
                          (S (ite (eq n xs_61_230) (S (count n xs_61_231)) (count n xs_61_231)))
                          ==.
                          -- add guard scrutinee =>
                          (S (ite g-34 (S (count n xs_61_231)) (count n xs_61_231)))
                          ==.
                          -- prop_52:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):g-13=True:xs_60=Z:xs_61=(Cons xs_61_230 xs_61_231):g-34=False =>
                          (S (ite False (S (count n xs_61_231)) (count n xs_61_231)))
                          ==.
                          -- prop_52:n=Z =>
                          (S (ite False (S (count Z xs_61_231)) (count n xs_61_231)))
                          ==.
                          -- lemma-(S (count Z ?xs_61))=(count Z (append ?xs_61 (Cons Z Nil))) =>
                          (S (ite False (count Z (append xs_61_231 (Cons Z Nil))) (count n xs_61_231)))
                          ==.
                          -- <= prop_52:n=Z
                          (S (ite False (count n (append xs_61_231 (Cons Z Nil))) (count n xs_61_231)))
                          ==.
                          -- <= prop_52:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):g-13=True:xs_60=Z
                          (S (ite False (count n (append xs_61_231 (Cons xs_60 Nil))) (count n xs_61_231)))
                          ==.
                          -- (ite False ?x ?y) =>
                          (S (count n xs_61_231))
                          ==.
                          -- prop_52:n=Z =>
                          (S (count Z xs_61_231))
                          ==.
                          -- lemma-(S (count Z ?xs_61))=(count Z (append ?xs_61 (Cons Z Nil))) =>
                          (count Z (append xs_61_231 (Cons Z Nil)))
                          ==.
                          -- <= prop_52:n=Z
                          (count n (append xs_61_231 (Cons Z Nil)))
                          ==.
                          -- <= prop_52:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):g-13=True:xs_60=Z
                          (count n (append xs_61_231 (Cons xs_60 Nil)))
                          ==.
                          -- <= (ite False ?x ?y)
                          (ite False (S (count n (append xs_61_231 (Cons xs_60 Nil)))) (count n (append xs_61_231 (Cons xs_60 Nil))))
                          ==.
                          -- <= prop_52:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):g-13=True:xs_60=Z:xs_61=(Cons xs_61_230 xs_61_231):g-34=False
                          (ite g-34 (S (count n (append xs_61_231 (Cons xs_60 Nil)))) (count n (append xs_61_231 (Cons xs_60 Nil))))
                          ==.
                          -- <= add guard scrutinee
                          (ite (eq n xs_61_230) (S (count n (append xs_61_231 (Cons xs_60 Nil)))) (count n (append xs_61_231 (Cons xs_60 Nil))))
                          ==.
                          -- <= (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys))
                          (count n (Cons xs_61_230 (append xs_61_231 (Cons xs_60 Nil))))
                          ==.
                          -- <= (append (Cons ?x ?xs) ?ys)
                          (count n (append (Cons xs_61_230 xs_61_231) (Cons xs_60 Nil)))
                          ==.
                          -- <= prop_52:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):g-13=True:xs_60=Z:xs_61=(Cons xs_61_230 xs_61_231)
                          (count n (append xs_61 (Cons xs_60 Nil)))
                          ==.
                          -- <= (rev (Cons ?x ?xs))
                          (count n (rev (Cons xs_60 xs_61)))
                          ==.

                          (count n (rev xs))
                          ***
                          QED
                        (True ) ->
                          -- 
                          (count n xs)
                          ==.
                          -- prop_52:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61) =>
                          (count n (Cons xs_60 xs_61))
                          ==.
                          -- (count ?x (Cons ?y ?ys)) =>
                          (ite (eq n xs_60) (S (count n xs_61)) (count n xs_61))
                          ==.
                          -- add guard scrutinee =>
                          (ite g-13 (S (count n xs_61)) (count n xs_61))
                          ==.

                          (ite True (S (count n xs_61)) (count n xs_61))

                          ==.

                          ==.
                          -- <= add guard scrutinee
                          (ite (eq n xs_61_230) (S (ite (eq n xs_60) (S (count n xs_61_231)) (count n xs_61_231))) (count n xs_61))
                          ==.
                          -- prop_52:n=Z =>

                          ==.

                          ==.
                          -- prop_52:n=Z:xs=(Cons xs_60 xs_61):g-13=True:xs_60=Z =>

                          ==.
                          -- <= prop_52:n=Z
                          (ite (eq n xs_61_230) (S (ite (eq n n) (count n (append xs_61_231 (Cons xs_60 Nil))) (count n xs_61_231))) (count n xs_61))
                          ==.

                          (ite (eq n xs_61_230) (S (ite (eq n n) (count Z (append xs_61_231 (Cons xs_60 Nil))) (count n xs_61_231))) (count n xs_61))

                          ==.
                          -- <= prop_52:n=Z
